. 1.Dustula allochana choppuna | | దుష్టుల ఆలోచన చొప్పున
Psalms -1.
Mubarak hai jo manta na salah shariron ki.
1. Dustula allochana choppuna naduvaka -
papulamaargamulayandu nilichiyundaka
2. Apahasinchunatti prajalu kurchundedu -
Aa chota kurchundaka yunduvaade dhanyudu
3. Yehovaa darmasastramandu anandinchuchu -
yallappudu dyanamu cheyuvade dhanyudu
4. Kaaluva neetiyora nathadu naatabadi thana -
kaalamuna phalinchu chettuvale yundunu
5. Aaku vadani chettuvale nathadundunu -
ayana cheyunadiyella saphalamagunu
6. Dhusta janulu a vidhamuga nundaka -
pottuvale gaaliki chedaragottabadudhuru
7. Nyaya vimarsa sabhalayandu dhustajanulu -
neetimantula sabhalo paapulunu niluvaru
8. Nethimanthula maargamu Yehova yerugunu
nadupunu dustula dhari nashanamunaku


. 2.Anyajanulela lechi galathu  || అన్యజనులేల లేచి - గల్లత్తు
Psalm - 2:1-10
Pallavi : Anyajanulela - lechi - galathu
Cheyu chunnaaru anya janulela
A.P. : Janamu lela - Vyardha maina
daani thalanchu chunnavi
1. Bhooloka raajulu - lechi -
Vaarekamugaa aalochinchi
Vaari paashamulanu thempi -
Paara veyuda manu chunnaaru “anya”
2. aakaasha vaasundu - vaarini -
apahasinchu chunnadu - navvi
vaaralatho palki kopamutho -
vaarini thalladilla cheyunu “anya”
3. Parishuddha - maina - naadu -
parvatha magu siyonu meeda
naaraaju naaseenunigaa Chesi -
yunnaanani selavitchenu “anya”
4. Kattada vivarinthu - naaku -
ittlu cheppenu Yehovaayanchu
Neevu naa kumaarundavu -
ninnu nenu kani yunnaanu “anya”
5. Nannu adugumu - neeku -
janamula bhoomini swaastyamugaa
diganthamula varaku
swaastyamugaa nosangedanu neeku “anya”
6. Inupa dandamutho - neevu -
vaarini naluga gottedavu
kundanu pagulagottu natlu
vaarini pagula gottedavu “anya”
7. Oh raajulaaraa - meeru -
jnaana vanthulai yundudi
oh bhoopathu laaraa - meeru -
naa bodha nondudi nede “anya”


. 3.Yehovaa maa prabhuvaa bhoomi || యెహోవా మా ప్రభువా
Psalm - 8
Pallavi : Yehovaa maa prabhuvaa bhoomi
aakaashamulo; mahima gala
nee naamamu goppadi
1. Paga theerchukonu shatruvunu maanpiveya -
baalura stuti stotramulatho; staapinchitivi nee voka
durgamu - ne daagu natlu aashraya durgamu “Yeho”
2. Nee chethi pani yaina aakaashamunu - chandra
nakshatramulane choodagaa - vaani darshinchi jnaapakamu
cheya - maanavundu epaativaadu “Yeho”
3. Neekante maanavuni konchemugaa - thakkuva
vaanigaa chesitivi - mahima prabhaava kireetamunu -
vaaniki dharimpa jesitivi “Yoho”
4. Adavi mrugamulu aakaasha pakshulu - samudra
mutsyamulu pashuvulu vaani paadamula krinda nunchi -
adhikaaramu vaanikitchitivi “Yoho”
5. Nee naamamu maa prabhuvaa Yehovaa - entho
ghanatha prabhaavamu galadi - aa naamamunu batti
maa kitchitivi - nee roopamunu maaku Halleluya “Yoho”


. 4.Stutinthun stutinthun naa kaalochana || స్తుతింతున్ స్తుతింతున్
Psalm-16:3-11
Mubarak, mubarak
Pallavi : Stutinthun - stutinthun - naa kaalochana
karthayagu devuni - raatrivelalo naa
antharindriyamu naaku nerpun “Stutin”
1. Naadu swaastya paaneeya bhaagamu - naa Yehovaa
neeve kaapaadedavu - manohara stalamulalo
paalu kalgenu - stutinthun “Stutin”
2. Shresta maino swaastyamu naaku kalgenu - sadaa
Kaalamu Yehovaa yandu naa; gurini nilpu chunnaanu -
gana nenu stutin tun “Stutin”
3. Naa kudi paarshya mandaayana yunnaadu - gaana
kadalchabada lenu ennadu; andu che naa hrudaya
maanandinchunu - Stutintun “Stutin”
4. Naa shareeramu surakshithamabugaa nivasinchu
chunnadi elananagaa nee parishudduni kullu
pattaniyaavu - Stutintun “Stutin”
5. Jeevamu gala nee maargamunu - neevu naakila
theliya jesedavu - neeve naa kshemmaa dhaaramani
ninnu - Stutintun “Stutin”
6. Sarvonnathudaa nee sannidhilo
sampooma santosha mentho galadu - nee kudi
chethilo nitya sukhamulu galavu - Stutintun “Stutin”


. 5.Yehovaa Naa Balamaa || యెహావా నా బలమా
Yehovaa Naa Balamaa
Yadhaarthamainadi Nee Maargam
Paripoornamainadi Nee Maargam (2)    ||Yehovaa||
Naa Shathruvulu Nanu Chuttinanoo
Narakapu Paashamularikattinanoo (2)
Varadavale Bhakthiheenulu Porlina (2)
Vadalaka Nanu Edabaayani Devaa (2)    ||Yehovaa||
Maranaputurulalo Maruvaka Moralida
Unnathadurgamai Rakshanasrungamai (2)
Thana Aalayamulo Naa Mora Vinenu (2)
Adarenu Dharani Bhayakampamuche (2)   ||Yehovaa||
Naa Deepamunu Veliginchuvaadu
Naa Cheekatini Veluguga Cheyunu (2)
Jalaraasulanundi Balamaina Chethitho (2)
Velupala Cherchina Balamaina Devudu (2)   ||Yehovaa||
Pourushamugala Prabhu Kopimpagaa
Parvathamula Punaadulu Vanakenu (2)
Thana Notanundi Vachchina Agni (2)
Dahinchivesenu Vairulanellan (2)                 ||Yehovaa||
Meghamulapai Aayana Vachchunu
Meghamulanu Thana Maatuga Jeyunu (2)
Urumula Merupula Menduga Jesi (2)
Apajayamichchunu Apavaadikini (2)             ||Yehovaa||
Dayagala Vaaripai Daya Choopinchunu
Katinulayedala Vikatamu Joopunu (2)
Garvishtula Yokka Garvamunanuchunu (2)
Sarvamu Nerigina Sarvaadhikaari (2)           ||Yehovaa||
Naa Kaallanu Ledi Kaalluga Jeyunu
Eththaina Sthalamulo Shakthitho Nilipi (2)
Rakshana Kedemu Naakandinchi (2)
Akshayamuga Thana Pakshamu Jerchina (2) ||Yehovaa||
Yehovaa Jeevamugala Devaa
Bahugaa Sthuthulaku Arhuda Neeve (2)
Anyajanulalo Dhanyatha Choopuchu (2)
Hallelooya Sthuthigaanamu Cheseda (2)   ||Yehovaa||


. 6.Yaakobu devudaapada kaalambula || యాకోబు దేవుడాపద కాలంబుల
Psalm - 20
Dukhon men sada teri Yahowa sune
Pallavi : Yaakobu devudaapada kaalambula
Yandu ninnudharinchi nee
Kuththaramunitchunu gaaka
1. Parishuddha stalamu nundi neeku
Saaya mitchunu - Siyonu nundi
Yehovaa ninnaadarinchunu “Yaakobu”
2. Nee naivedyamu lanni jnapti nunchu
konuchu nee dahana balulanu
angeekarinchunu gaaka “Yaakobu”
3. Nee korika siddhimpajesi nee
Yaalochana-yanthatini saphalamu
chesi ninnu gaachunu “Yaakobu”
4. Nee rakshananu batti memu
Yutsahintumu maa devuni naamamuna
dhwajamu neththedamu “Yaakobu
5 Nee prardhana lanni Yehovaa
saphala parachunu - yehovaa thana
abhishikhtuni rakshinchunu gaaka “Yaakobu”
6. Rakshinchi dakshina hasta balamunu
choopunu - yuttara mitchunu
parishuddha stalamu nundi “Yaakobu”
7. Atishaya paduduru radha
gurramulatho yehovaa naamamulo
manamu athishayinthumu “Yaakobu”
8. Vaaru krungi nela meeda padi
leva kunnaaru - manamulechi
chakka gaa niluchu chunnaamu “Yaakobu”


. 7.Naadu devaa naadu devaa || నాదు దేవా నాదు దేవా
Psalm-22:1-10
Mere Khuda mere Khuda
Pallavi : Naadu devaa naadu devaa -
nannela vidanaadithi vayyaa
A. P. : Nannu rakshimpaka aartha dwani -
vinaka neevela doora munnaavu “Naadu”
1. Raatrimbagallu morra bettagaa - ela uttara meeya
kunnaavu - Ishraayelu stotramu pai koorchunna -
parishudda devudavai yunnaavu “Naadu”
2. Maa pitarulu nee yandu viswasinchagaa rakshinchitivi
moralidi ninnu nammiri vidudalondi
siggu nonda ledu “Naadu”
3. Narudanu kaanu purugunu - narulache nindimpa
badithi narulache thruneekaaramu pondi yunna
vaada Naithini “Naadu”
4. Nannu joochu vaarellaru - thama pedavulanu
virichi thalala naadinchu chunnaaru -
nannapahasinchu chunnaaru “Naadu”
5. Yehovaapai bhaara munchumu - thaanu ninnu
vidipinchu nemo - vaadaayana kistudu kaadaa
vaani thappinchu nemo yanduru “Naadu”
6. Garbhamu nundi nan deesina vaadaa - naa thalli yodda
stanya paanamu, cheyu chundagaa neevekadaa -
naaku nammika puttinchitivi “Naadu”
7. Garbaha vaasi nainadi modalu - nundi naa
kaadhaaramu neeve - nannu dalli kanina naati nundi
naa devudavu neevu “Naadu”


. 8.Yehovaa naa kaapari || యెహోవా నా కాపరి
Psalm - 29
Yahowa mera charwaha hai
Pallavi : Yehovaa naa kaapari - lemi kalugadu
pachchikalapai parunda jeyu chunnaadu
1. Shaanti karambagu sheresta jalamula - chentha
nannadi pinchu chunnaadu “Yeho”
2. Sarvadaa naadu praanambunaku - seda
deerchu chunnaadu Yehovaa “Yeho”
3. Thana naamamunu batti neethi maargamulo -
nannu chakkagaa nadupu chunnadu “Yeho”
4. Cheekati loyalo ne thiriginanu - etti
apaayamunaku bhayapadanu “Yeho”
5. Nee duddu karra nee dandamuthona
naadarinchi thodai yunduvu “Yeho”
6. Naa shatruvula yeduta neevu naaku
bhojanamu siddaparachuduvu “Yeho”
7. Noonetho naathala nanti yunnaavu -
naa ginne nindi poruluchunnadi “Yeho”
8. Nannu ventaadu sadaa krupa kshemamu
nityamehovaa mandiramulo nundeda “Yeho”


. 9.Neeve Yehovaa naa kaaparivi || నీవే యెహోవా నా కాపరివి
Psalm - 23:1-6
Tu his Yahowa mera charwaha
Pallavi : Neeve Yehovaa naa kaaparivi
naakemi koduva ledilalona
1. Pachikagala chotla nanu jerchi - swachcha -
magu jalamu thraagaanitchi naa praanamunaku sedanu
deerchi - nannu nadupumu neethi maargamuna“Neeve”
2. Gaadhaandha kaara loyala yandu - padi yundi nenu
sacharinchinanu - thodai yunduvu - nee duddu karra
dandamutho nee vaadarinchedavu “Neeve”
3. Shatruvula yeduta neevu naaku - nityamagu vindu
sidda parachi - naa thala noonetho nanti yunnaavu -
naa ginne nindi porluchunnadi “Neeve”
4. Nishchayamugaa krupaa kshemamule - vachchu
naaventa ne brathuku dinamul - chira kaalamu
Yehovaa mandiramuna - Stiramugaa ne nivasinchedanu “Neeve”


. 10.Yehovaa naa kaapari naaku lemi ledu || యెహోవా నా కాపరి నాకు లేమి లేదు
Psalm-23:1-6
Yahowa charwaha mera
Pallavi : Yehovaa naa kaapari naaku lemi ledu
patchika gala chotla machikatho nadupun
1. Maranapu cheekatilo thirugu chundinanu
Prabhu Yesu nannu karunatho aadarinchun “Yeho”
2. Paga vaari yeduta prematho noka vindu
prabhu siddamu cheyun paravasha mondedanu “Yeho”
3. Noonetho naa thalanu abhiskekamu cheyun
naa hrudayamu nindi porluchunnadi “Yeho”
4. Chirakaalamu nenu prabhu mandiramulo
vasiyincheda niratham santhasamugaanundun “Yeho”


. 11.Yesu prabhoo kapari naaku || యేసు ప్రభూ కాపరి నాకు
Psalm - 23:1
Yishu mera Cherwaha main
Pallavi : Yesu prabhoo kapari naaku - vaasigaa stutinchedan
Yesu gorrepillanu - Poyedanu thanaventa
1. Pachika patlaku - machikato nadupun - swatcha
jalamuchenta - nitchunu vishraanti - mundu mundu
velluchu - pondugaa rakshinchu nannu;
thana maadhurya swarambuna - thanivi deerchunu“Yesu”
2. Marana loya dwaaraa sarigaa nadipinchunu - adavi
bhayamu lella - edabaapi rakshinchun - haththi oththi
katti gaayaa lentho aadarinchunu - vintagu aayana
prema sevalo santoshinthunu “Yesu”
3. Shatrula mundaaharam samsiddamu jeyunu -
naa ginne nindinchi - porli paara jesi-kadigi kadigi
shuddhi chesi - aatma daana mitchenu; vadigaa
aayana saayamuna - jayamuna velledanu “Yesu”


. 12.Bhoomiyu daani sampoornatha lokamu || భూమియు దాని సంపూర్ణత లోకము
Psalm - 24:1-10
Prabhu Yishu Raja hai
Pallavi : Bhoomiyu daani sampoornatha lokamu
daani nivaasulehovaave
1. aayana samudramu meeda daaniki
punaadi vesenu - pravaaha jalamula meeda
daanini stira parachenu “bhoomiyu”
2. Yehovaa parvathamunaku nekka dagina
vaadevvadu-yehovaa parshudda
stalamulo niluva dagina vaadevvadu “bhoomiyu”
3. Vyardha maina daani yandu manassu
pettakayu-nirdhosha chetulu shuddha
hrudayamu kaligina vaade “bhoomiyu”
4. Ninnashrayinchi nee sannidhini
vedakedi vaadu-vaadaasheervaadamu
neethi - matvamu nondunu “bhoomiyu”
5. gummamu laaraa Mee Paikethudi Puratana thalupular
mahima gala raaju praveshinchunatlu
mimmunu leva neththu konudi “bhoomiyu”
6. Mahima gala ee raajevadu balashouryamu
gala prabhuve - Yuddha shoorudaina
Yehovaa paraakramamu gala prabhuve “bhoomiyu”
7. Mahima gala ee raajevadu sainyamula
Yehovaaye - aayane ee mahima gala
raaju Halleluyaa aamen “bhoomiyu”


. 13.Devaa nee mukhamunu naaku || దేవా నీ ముఖమును నాకు
Psalm-27:9-14
Yahowa Apne mukh ko
Pallavi : Devaa nee mukhamunu naaku
daachakumu - naa prabhuvaa
nee sevakuni kopamuche -
throsi veyaku Yehovaa
1. Devaa naa rakshana kartha - neeve naa - sahayudavu
nannu diganaada valadu-nannu viduvakumu “Devaa”
2. Naadu thalidandrulu - nannu vidichinanu
naa devundagu Yehovaa nannu-cheradeeyunu “Devaa”
3. Naakai ponchi yunnatti vaarini choochi nannu
saraala daarini nadupu - manchi
margamu bodinchu “Devaa”
4. Naapai lechi yunnaru - abadda saakshulu kroorul
nannappaginchaku devaa-naadu virodhulaku “Devaa”
5. Yehovaa daya pondedanu - sajeevula - deshamuna
itti nammakamuleni-yedala-ne nemagudunu “Devaa”
6. Dhairyamu thechukoni - nibbara hrudayamu galgi
Yehovaa devuni koraku - kanipettukoni yundumu “Devaa”


. 14.Udaya saayanthramula nella velala prabhuvaa ||  ఉదయ సాయంత్రముల నెల్లవేళల ప్రభువా
Psalm - 27:1
Subah aur sham aur har samay
Pallavi : Udaya saayanthramula nella velala prabhuvaa -
ne dyaaninchi paadedan, parishuddudu, parishuddudu
parishuddundani dootalupaaduta vinabaduchundun
1. Yehovaaye naaku velugu rakshanayu - ne nevariki
verathunu Yehovaaye naa praana durgambaaye -
Shatruvulu thotrilliri “Udaya”
2. Yuddamu cheyutaku dandudiginanu - naa hrudayamu bhayapadadu
yuddamu reginanu deeni yandu
ne - dhairyamu vidivakundun “Udaya”
3. Yehovaa yodda varamokkatadigitini - daanini vedakuchunnaanu
Yehovaa prasannatha Juchi- aalayamuna - dhyaninchutaye naa aasha
“Udaya”
4. Thana parna shaalalalo nanu jerchi kaachunu - naa aapatkaalamu nandu
thana gudaaramulona nanu
daachi yunchunu - durgamupai nekkinchun “Udaya”
5. Naa sannidi vediki naa swaramu vinumani - neevu palkitivi gaana
nee sannidini vedaki nee swarame venedanu -
nee samukhamunu daachaku “Udaya”
6. Naa thalli dandrulu nannu vidachinanu - Yehovaaye cheradeeyun
ne dhairyamu kaligi nibbaramuga
nundeda - nee koraku kanipettedan “Udaya”
7. Yehovaa naakai yuddeshinchinadi - aayanaye
neraverchunu - mahonnathuni maataku bhaya padedi
parishuddula - korikalu neraverchunu “Udaya”


. 15.Yehovaa naa devaa nityamu || యెహోవా నా దేవా నిత్యము

He Prabhu Yahowa sarwada
Pallavi : Yehovaa naa devaa nityamu
nenu ninnu stutiyincheda
Halleluya - Halleluya - Halleluya - Halleluya
1. Yehovaa naa shatruvulanu - naa pai santoshimpa - neeyaka
neevu nannudharinchi nandukai nenu - ninnu koni yaadu chunnaanu
“Yehovaa”
2. Nenu neeku morra petta gaa - neevu nan - swasta parachitivi
parishudda jnaapakaardha - naamamunu batti
bhakhtulaaraa - prabhun keertinchudi “Yehovaa”
3. Yehovaa paataalamu lo nundi naapraanamu - leva deesitivi
nenu samaadhiloki diga kundaga - neevu nannu brathikinchitivi
“Yehovaa”
4. aayana kopamu nimishame - daya aayushkaala - mundunu
edpu vachchi raatri yundina - Udaya - muna santoshamu kalugunu
“Yehovaa”
5. Ne nennadu kadalanani - naa - kshema kaalamuna thalachiti
Yehovaa daya kaligi neeve naa - parvathamu stira parachitivi
“Yehovaa”
6. Nee mukhamu neevu daachina yapudu nenu kshobhilliti
Yehovaa neeke mora pettithini - naa prabhuvunu brathi maalu kontini
“Yehovaa”
7. Nenu samaadhiloki digina - naa praanamu - valana
laabhamaa mannu ninnu - Stutinchunaa ?
nee satyamunu goorchi adi vivarinchu naa ? “Yehovaa”
8. Naa angalaarpunu neeve gaa - naatyamugaa -
maarchi yuntivi naa gone patta vidipinchi
santosha - vastramu dharimpa jesitivi “Yehovaa”


. 16.Yavvani athikramamulu mannimpabaduno || ఎవ్వని అతిక్రమములు మన్నింపబడెనో
Psalm - 32:1-8
Dhanya hai wah jiske kshama Hue apradh
Pallavi : Yavvani athikramamulu mannimpabaduno
paapa parihaara mevadondeno vaade dhanyudu
1. Yehovaache nirdhoshigaa theercha badiyu - aatmalo
Kapatamu lenivaade dhanuyudu “Yavvani”
2. Mounivai yundina dinamella nejesi natti
aarthadwaniche naa yemukalu ksheeninchenu “Yavvani”
3. Divaaraatrul nee cheyi naa pai baruvai yunda
naa saaramu vesavilo yendinatlaaye “Yavvani”
4. Nenu naa doshamunu kappu konaka nee
yeduta naa papamunu oppukontini “Yavvani”
5. Nee sannidhi naa paapamula noppukonagaa
neevu naa doshamunu manninchitivigaa “Yavvani”
6. Kaavuna nee darshana kaalamandu
bhakhtigala vaaru ninnu praardhinchedaru “Yavvani”
7. Vistaara jala pravaahamulu porlinanu
nishchyamuga navi vaari meediki raavu “Yavvani”
8. naaku daagu chotu neeve shramalo nundi
neevu nannu rakshinchedavu naadu durgamaa “Yavvani”
9. Vimochana gaanamulatho neevu nannu
aavarinchi naa kupadeshamu chesedavu “Yavvani”


. 17.Sannuthinthu neppudehovaanu || సన్నుతింతు నెప్పుడెహోవాను
Psalm-34:1-10
Sada Prabhu ko dhanya kahun main
Pallavi : Sannuthinthu neppudehovaanu -
thana keerti naa nota nundunu
1. Athishayinthu nehovaanu batti -
Santhoshinthuru deenulu vini “Sannut”
2. Ghana parachudi devuni peru -
goppa cheyudamu ekamugaa “Sannut”
3. Thana yodda ne vichaarinchagaa -
thappinche nannu bhayamula nundi “Sannut”
4. Thananu choodaga velgu kaligenu -
thama mukhamulu lajjimpa kunde “Sannut”
5. Yehovaa bhaktulandari chuttu -
doota kaavali yundi rakshinchu “Sannut”
6. Devuduthamudani ruchi choodu -
dhanyudu thannaashrainchuvaadu “Sannut”
7. Aakaleththu simphapu pillalaku -
aashrithula kemi koduva ledu “Sannut”


. 18.Pillalara na mata vinudi || పిల్లలారా నా మాట వినుడి
Psalms - 34:11-18
Ao bachchon suno Main sunaun
Pallavi : Pillalara na mata vinudi -
yehovayandu bakthi nerpedanu
1. Brathuka goruvaadevadaina kaladaa -
melunonduchu chaalaa dinamulu “Pillalara”
2. Kapatamaina chedumatalaadaka -

vini sramalanundi thappinchunu “Pillalara”
7. Viriginatti hrudhayamulaku -
Yehova aasannudai yunnaadu “Pillalara”
8. Naligiyunna vaarala nella -
ayane rakshinchu premagalgi “Pillalara”

. 34.Yoodaalo devudu prasiddhudu || యూదాలో దేవుడు ప్రసిద్ధుడు

“Yooda”

nidra nondi yunnaaru - paraakrama shaalu landarini vaari
bahu balamunu harinchenu - yaakobu devaa needu
gaddimpunaku - radha saaradhula kashwamulaku nidra kalgenu “Yooda”
3. Neeve bhayankarudavu devaa - neevu kopa padu vela

rakshinchi nyaayamu theerchanu lechu naadu bhoomi bhayamu nondi oorako yundunu “Yooda”
4. Narula kopamu ninnu stutinchunu - vaari aagraha

mrokku ballu chellinchudi - thana chuttu kaanukalu
arpinchavalenu - adhikaarula garva manachiveyu
vaadu - bhoo raajulaku aayana bheekarudu “Yooda”


. 35.Devuniki morra pettudunu elugeththi || దేవునికి మొఱ్ఱపెట్టుదును ఎలుగెత్తి

prabhu vinkennatikini katakshamunchadaa

anukonutaku naa shramale kaaranamu

thalanchukondu naadu manassulo nippudu

nee kriyalanu dhyaanamu ne jesikondunu

mahaa devaa neevanti vaadu ekkadunnaadu
11. Aashcharya kriyalu jariginchu devudavu neeve
janamulalo prabhaavamunu choopi yannavu


. 36.Mana balamaina yaakobu devuniki || మన బలమైన యాకోబు దేవునికి

ninnu - rappinchina Yehovaa devudanu “Mana”

7. Ayyo Ishrayelu neevu naa maata - vinina pakshaana
entha melagu anya devathala nevvarikini - neevu
ennadu pooja cheya raadu “Mana”

. 41.Mahonnathuni chaatuna vasinchu vaade || మహోన్నతుని చాటున వసియించువాడే

nee daasuniki melu chesi yunnavu

kartha neeve naaku bodha cheyumu
nee yaajnalandu nammika nunchitini “Yeho”
2. Naaku shrama kalugaka munupu - naa devaa
nenu throva veeditini nedu nee maata
nera verchu chunnaanu “Yeho”
3. Deva neevu dayagala vaadavu - devaa
neevu melu cheyu chunnaavu - nee kattadala
naaku bodhinchumu “Yeho”
4. Garvistulu naaku Verodamuga
kalpinetu durenoo Abadamulu
nee yunadesamu lanesarinthunu “Yeho”
5. Vaari hrudayamu Kerovuu vale - ohaala mandam
gaanai yunnavp-aagnyalalo
aanandinchu ununavu “Yeho”
6. Devaa nenu needu kattadalanu
nerchukonu natlu shramala nondi
yunduta naaku yentho melaayenu “Yeho”
7. Velaadi vendi naanemula kante
velaadi bangaaru naanemula kante
neevitchina aajnalu naaku melu “Yeho”


. 53.Naa shramalo Yehovaaku moraliditini || నా శ్రమలో నేను యెహోవాకు మొఱలిడితిని

baanamula neepai veyunu “Naa shrama”

yunnaanu - kedaaru gudaramula
yodda kaapura munnaanu “Naa shrama”

nenu korunadi samaadhaaname “Naa shrama”

. 55.Yehovaa mandiramunaku velludamani  || యెహోవా మందిరమునకు వెళ్లుదమని

. 64.Halleluya naa pranamaa || హల్లెలూయ నా ప్రాణమా

“Halle”
3. Vaari praanamu nashiyinchunu - vaaru mantilo galisedaru
vaari sankalpamulanniyu nee diname naashanano nondun “Halle”

. 65.Devuniki stotramu gaanamu || దేవునికి స్తోత్రము గానము

keertinchumu koni yaadumu-aanandinchu vaadani “Devuniki”
10. Pillala naasheervadinchiyu - bala parache nee gummamul

. 68.Yehovaaku stutulu paadandi - meeru samaja || యెహోవాకు స్తుతులు పాడండి - మీరు

. 69.Yehovaaku krotha keerthana || యెహోవాకు క్రొత్త కీర్తన పాడుడి

. 90.Aanada maananda mayenu || ఆనందమానంద మాయెను

. 125.Prabhuva nee goppa thanamu || ప్రభువా నీ గొప్పతనము

O raja neeke nityaghanata khyathi galgunu

. 165.Sannuthinchedanu ellappudu || సన్నుతించెదను ఎల్లప్పుడు

Har samay stuti karta rahunga

aayana keerti naa nota nundu
1. Yehovaaku praardhincha gaa - naa bhayamantha
tholaginchenu - shrama lannitilo naatho nundi (2)
chera deesi nannu aadarinche - aaraadincheda
nellappudu “Sannu”
2. Jeevitha manthaa paadu chundunu - nee
melulaku oh prabhuvaa - naa aayushkaala
manthayunu (2) nee vishwaasyatha
kora keppudu - nirathamu ninnu stotrinthu “Sannu”

prabhaavamu gala prabhuvaa - thanivi

kaaryamulakai - thappaka ninnu stutiyinthu “Sannu”
4. Nee sankalpamunu neraverchi - nadipinchitivi

. 184.Yesu prabhuve saataanu || యేసు ప్రభువే సాతాను

thana raajyamunandu manalanu jerchun

mana vijayamu Yeseyani harshinchedamu “Yesu”
3. Manalanentho preminchenu

sarveswarundaa neeke jayamu “Yesu”
4. Mana maayana sanghamugaa
thana rakhtamu dwaaraa samakoorchenu
sanghamunaku shirassaayane
saagilapadi mrokki aaraadinchedamu “Yesu”
5. Mahonnathudu mahaaghanudu
mahima raaju manaku vijayamunitche
maranamu gelchi thirigi leche
aarbhaatamutho manamu harshinchedamu “Yesu”

ninnu poojintunu - manasaara ninne
keertintunu - aaraadhanalaku yogyudavu
1. Bhariyinchitivi naa rogomulan - bhariyinchitivi
naa vyasanamulan - arigitivi naakai caluvariki -
pariharinchitivi paapa sikshan “Aaradhana”
2. Naa yatikramamulakai gaayapadi - naa
doshamulakai kottabadi - chindina siluva
rakhtamulo naa daaridrayamu tholaginchitivi “Aaradhana”
3. Nashiyinchina nanu vedakitivi - nashiyinchina
nanu lepitivi - naa shaapamunu choopinchitivi
nee shaantamutho kshaminchitivi “Aaradhana”


. 202.Stotrinchedamu daiva  || స్తోత్రించెదము దైవకుమారుని
STUTHI - (PRAISE)
Psalm - 40:2

1. Stotrinchedamu daiva kumaaruni - noothana
jeevamutho nirantharamu maarani raajunu
ghanambu cheyudamu
Pallavi : Yesu maa rakshakudu kalmashamu
leni vaadu samasthamunu kaligina
yesu prabhunake Halleluya
2. Bhayankara maina bheethini golpedu jigata
oobinundi balamaina hastamutho nannu
eththi bandapai stira parachen “Yesu”
3. Kanu paapaga nanu kaayu prabhundu kunukadu
nidrinchadu - thana chetilo nanu chekkina
prabhuvunu cheri stutinchedamu “Yesu”
4. Thalli dandriyu yeda baapinanu - viduvaka
kaayunu - ellappudu nenu bhajihinchedanu
vallabhu desu prabhun “Yesu”
5. Aatmeeya poraatamunaku prabhuvu aatma
shakti nitchen - stutiyu neeke ghanatayu
neeke - yuga yugamula Iona “Yesu”

kramamugaa krupache saagedamu “Krupa”

ika jeevinchuta naa prabhu korake

pennugaa nerpunu Halleluya “Krupa”

. 217.Bhakhtulaaraa smariyinchedamu || భక్తులారా స్మరియించెదము

odinche inthavarakunu aadukonenugaa -

sandhinchutakai, - ganuka manamu naduchukonedamu

. 221.Prabhaava shaktulu || ప్రభావ శక్తులు

Praise to the Lord, the Almighty
1. Prabhaava shaktulu kalgina raajunutimpu
deeni priyaatma ! korudu reni smarimpu
koodudido ! kinnera veenelatho
gaanamu cheyanulendi
2. Sarvamu vinthaga - paalana chesedu vaadu
rekkalatho ninu mosenu gaavuna baadu
neeku sadaa - kaavali yundu gadaa -
daani grahimpavadela
3. Aatmanu! mikkili vinthagaa ninnu srujinchi
soukyamu nitchuchu snehamutho nadipinchi
kastamulo - kappuchu - rekkalatho -
gaachina naadhunuthimpu
4. Snehapu varshamu - neepai thaa guriyinchi
andaru choochuchu undagane karuninchi
deevenalu - neeku nirathamu -
nitchina naadhunuthimpu
5. Naadhuni naamamu - naathma ! Smarinchi
nuthimpu oopiri galagina swaramaa - neevu
nuthimpu - sanghamulo nabraham santatitho -
naadhu nuthimpumu


. 222.Yesu prabhoo nee  || యేసు ప్రభు నీ
John - 6:35
Prabhuji Tere chehere ko
Pallavi : Yesu prabhoo nee mukha darshanamuche
naa prati yaashanu theerchukondunu
1. Neeve naaku jeevaahaaramu ninnu sameepinchu
vaaremaatramu aakali gonarila
aadarshudavu “Yesu”
2. Nee mandira samrudhi valana naa madi
nepudu thrupti ponditini aananda
jalamunu thraaginchu chunnaavu “Yesu”
3. Neeve naaku jeevapu maargamu nee
sannidhini poornaanandam kaladani
ninnu ghana parachedanu “Yesu”
4. Aashatho nindina naa praanamunu
aakaligonina naadu aatmanu melutho
neevu thrupti parachitivi “Yesu”
5. Nee santoshamu naa kosagitivi naa
santoshamu paripoornamugaa kaavalayunani
korina prabhuvaa “Yesu”
6. Naa jeevitha kaalamanthayunu nee
aalayamulo nivasinchuchu Halleluya
paatanu paadeda prabhuvaa “Yesu”


. 223.Jayamani paadu jayamani || జయమని పాడు జయమని

parachi nirdhoshuluga theerche “Jaya”
3. Yesulo mammu rakhtamu dwaaraa
vimochinchitivi - yentho krupatho mammunu
kadigi manninchi naavugaa “Jaya”

baapegaa - vaasiga marana balamu
tholaginchi paapamu baapegaa “Jaya”
5. Kristulo mammu nootana parachi thandrini
thelipenu - karuninchi mammu angeekarinche
entho adbuthamu “Jaya”
6. Maa swaastyamunaku sanchakaruvugaa
aatma mudra nitchenu - mano netramulu
veliginchi maaku goppa nireekshana nitche “Jaya”
7. Prabhu kristulo vaadabaarani swaastyamuga
naitimi - parishuddulalo mahimaishwaryambu
yentho goppadi “Jaya”

. 225.Krupaathi shayamul  || కృపాతిశయముల్

Halleluya - stotramulatho - keertinthu nityamu


. 226.Stutinchu stutinchu || స్తుతించు - స్తుతించు

ninnu nirminchi roopambu nichina srustikartayane (2)
jeevapu data ayane nee rakshana kartayane (2)
1. Preminchenu ninnu ayane - saaswata premache
erparachu kone ninnu - bhoomi puttakamunupe devude
nararupiyaye - ayana peru Yesu prabhu -2- ayana
“Stutinchu”
2. Yakobunu srujiyinche - Israyeluku rupuniche
neeku todaiyundun - bayapadakumani palike
peru petti pilichi - na sottu nee vanenu - naa sottu nevanenu
“Stutinchu”
3. Preminchi nannu rakshinche - stuti chellinchi pujintun
tana rupamu naku niche - aradinchi ganaparatun
paraloka pouruniga chesen - hrudayarpana narpintun -
hrudayarpana narpintun “Stutinchu”
4. Sahavasamulo nilichi - pratyakshata yandundi
emi sambavinchinanu - prabhu pakshamu nundavalen
antamandu bahumanamittun - ani prabhuve cheppenugaa
“Stutinchu”


. 227.Ne sthuthinchedanu yesu namamunu || నే స్తుతించెదను యేసు నామమును

“Nesthuthi”

Ye papamerugani aa pavanudu – sapagrahiyai chavondenu
“Nesthuthi”
3. Sodhana kalamula yanduna – vedana kalamula yanduna

“Nesthuthi”

. 228.Padeda deva  nee krupalan || పాడెద దేవా - నీ కృపలన్
Pallavi : Padeda deva – nee krupalan
Nuthana geethamulan – sthothramu chellinthun
Sthuthi sthothramu chellinthun (2)
1. Bhumi punadulu veyakamunde yesulo chesithivi (2)
Prema punadulu vesithivi deenuni brochithivi
Ee deenuni brochithivi “Pade”
2. Pravimala rakthamu kaluvari siluvalo kalunaku nitchithivi (2)
Prema krupa mahadaiswaryamulatho paapamu thudichithivi
Na papamu thudichithivi “Pade”
3. Papamu sapamu narakapu vedana mari tholaginchithivi
Aparadhamulache chachina nanudhara brathikinchithivi
Nannu brathikinchithivi “Pade”
4. Devuni rajyapu varasudanuga kristhulo chesithivi
Cheekati rajyapu sakthula nundi nanu vidipinchithivi
Chera nanu vidipinchithivi “Pade”
5. Mudrinchithivi suddathmatho nannu bhadramu chesithivi
Satya swaroopa nitya nivasi sottuga chesithivi
Nee sotthuga chesithivi “Pade”
6. Anyudanai ninnu yerugaka yunnanu dhanyuni chesithivi
Priya pattana powrula sevimpanu varamula nosagithivi
Krupa varamula nosagithivi “Pade”

Keerthinthunu nee naamam – ghanaparathunu – nee naamam
O ma prabhuva rammu eevulatho – mammu
naseervadimpa “Yesu”

O ma prabhuva rammu eevulatho – mammu naseervadimpa
“Yesu”

1. Dayaamayundagu thandrivi neeve - thallini minchina
daatavu neeve - mayaa mamathala gaadhala nundi
mammulanu rakshinchitivi “Maa devaa”
2. Kodi pillalanu kaasedu pagidi - aapadalanninti
baapithi vayyaa sarva kaalamula yanduna neeke -
chakkaga samstutulagu neeke “Maa devaa”
3. Simhapu pillalu aakali gonina - simhapu bonulo
nanu vesinanu - siggu kaluga kundaga nanu neevu -
gaapaadu chunna vee ilalo “Maa devaa”
4. Maranaloya landuna ne nunna - tharunamulu naaku
virodhamaina - charanamul paadedu vidhamuna neevu -
nannorchu chunnaavugaa “Maa devaa”
5. Vyaadhulu nannu baadhinchi nanu - vyaakulamulu
hrudayamulo nunna vadalavu nannila anaadhuniga
neppudu nanu brochuchu nunduvugaa “Maa devaa”
6. Needu satya maakaashamu kante - athyunnathamuga
staapincha bade needu satyamunu neechudanagu
naa kanulaku pratyaksha parachitivi “Maa devaa”
7. Parvathambulu tholagina gaani - palu vidhakondalu
thatharillinanu paavanudaa needu vela leni yatti
krupa nanu viduvadu Halleluyaa “Maa devaa”


. 240.Yehovaa goppa kaaryamulu || యెహోవా గొప్ప కార్యములు

. 244.Devuni keertinchedamu || దేవుని కీర్తించెదము - దైవపుత్రుని

. 253.Devuni stutincharandi || దేవుని స్తుతించ రండి

3. Needu mandirambulo - melu cheta mammunu
thruptiparachina prabhu - stutulu neeke chellunu“Stutu”
4. Needu naama ghanathanu - needu prema panulanu
naadhudaa ne paadeda - naadu priya prabhuvaa “Stutu”
5. Satyaroopi neevegaa - sakala srusti karthavu
satatamu mammelumu - Halleluya paadedam “Stutu”

. 314.Prakaasha vastramutho paraloka mahimatho  || ప్రకాశ వస్త్రముతో పరలోక మహిమతో

vaarini - devuni prajalanu thana chenthan jerchun “Raajula”
3. Dhanyulu prabhukai joochedi vaaru - minnuna prabhutho
kalisi velledaru - viswasulanu prematho prabhuvu -
aahwaaninchunu thana sannidiki “Raajula”
4. Anantha jeevamu nee kitchunu - ghanatha mahima prabhu
neekitchun - thandritho ninnu jerchunu prabhuvu -
jeeva kireetamu neekitchunu “Raajula”

1. Papamunaku jeetamu maranamu O papi bhayapadavaa ?
chuchunadella nasinchu nishchayamu - chudanide nityamu
Pallavi : Yesurajuvachunu inka kontakaalame -
mokshamandu cherudumu
2. Lokasukhamu nammaku nammaku - aa ichchalu maayamagu
nee jeevamu povu samayamuna-chilligawa venttaraadu “Yesu”
3. Nee kaalamella vyaradamaguchunnadi - lokamayalayanduna
daivakopamu vachutaku munddu - nee rakshkuni cherumu “Yesu”
4. Daiva prema paruchunnadi - kalvarigiri meedanundi
nee papamella andupovunu - snanambu chesinan “Yesu”
5. Maha papinaina nannunu naa mitrudangikarinchen
O paapi neevu parugidiraa - deva deevenala pondumu “Yesu”
6. Kashtadukkamu lekkuvagucho - Istudesuni veedanu
sigguleka cherudu nayanachentha-neppudu vasintunu “Yesu”


. 338.Parugidara sodaruda  ||    పరుగిడిరా సోదరుడా
Isiah - 55:6
Parugidara sodaruda
Pallavi : Parugidara sodaruda - prabhu sannidi neevu jerutakai
1. Yugasamaptiki aagamanamunaku -
suchanalenno choodumuraa
vedanalenno meediki vachchuraa -
kalavaramondaka kanipettumura “Paru”
2. Indlanu gattuchu pendliki ichchuhu -
naarunu naatuchu traaguchu tinuchu
jagamulo janulu digulu lenappudu -
dongavale ila doravai vachura “Paru”
3. Aa dinamainanu aa gadiyainanu -
paramuna dootalu dharanilo manujulu
yevarunugaani erugane erugaru -
melakuvatho Yesu pilupunu vinuchu “Paru”
4. Aa dinamula sharma anthamu kaagaa -
suryuni chandruni chikati kammu
akasamandali shaktulu kadalunu -
mahimato Yesu immahidiguraa “Paru”
5. Arbaatamutho aashcharyamutho -
devuni bhoorato mana prabhu digura
kristu nandunna mrutulaguvaaru -
ekamuga prabhu Yesuni jera “Paru”
6. Yetuchuchina neekatu kanipinchunu -
kondala bandala nundinanu
kodama simhamai kopagniyai -
yeduruga vachina kadalaga levura “Para”
7. Eththabaduta kayathamaa neevu -
tarunamu idiyethadavu cheyakura
rakshanalo nireekshana kaligi -
rakshaku desuni rajyamu chera “Para”


. 339.Vinudi sodarulaaraa  || వినుడి సోదరులారా
I Timothy -1:15
Sun lo mere bhaiyo masihji mera
Pallavi : Vinudi sodarulaaraa - na Yesu prabhu ilaketenchen
1. Ilaketenchen - mukthini dechchen
papula vidipinchen - vidipinchanesu ilaketenchen “Vinu”
2. Swargeeya thandriki - eka kumaarudu
manushya putrundayan - putrunduga ilaketenchen “Vinu”
3. Gruddiki kannulu - moogaki maatalu
chevitiki chevulanichen - ichutakesu ilaketenchen “Vinu”
4. Kustu rogula - shuddula jesenu
chachina vaarini lepen - leputakesu ilaketenchen “Vinu”
5. Paapamulo neevu - padiyundagaa
pavitra premanu jupen - jupenchanesu ilkaetenchen “Vinu”
6. Paapula korakai - siluvanu mosen
raktamunu chindhinchen-chindincha nesu ilaketenchen “Vinu”
7. Yesu naamamuna - viswaasa munchumu
nischayamuga rakshinchun - rakshinchanesu ilaketenchen “Vinu”
8. Mahima ghanatha - mayesu prabhunake
mammula thandritho jerchen jerchutakesu ilaketenchen “Vinu”


. 340.Randi randi rayamuna Yesuni  ||  రండి రండి రయమున యేసుని
John - 3:16
Randi randi rayamuna
Pallavi : Randi randi rayamuna Yesuni -
rakshakuniga nangeekarinchudi
A. P. : Preethito prabhuni cherudi prabhula prabhuve
raajula raajuve raabovu naathade
1. Prayasapadi bharamu moyuvarala -
athi prematho nahvaaninchenu
bharamantha paradrolunu, vishrnatinichunu
vegame rarammu eemaata nikkamu “Randi”
2. Papapu jeetamu nithya narakamu, papi neekika dikkevaru
nitya jeeva miyyavachenu, nee koraku vachchenu
thana praanamichenu, ninnu rakshimpanu “Randi”
3. Mayalokam mosamujesenu -
marana samayamu samipinchenu
thannu cheruvari nevvarin, truneekarinchadu
ninu throsiveyadu ee maata nammu “Randi”
4. Kristu Yesu ninu preminchi nee korakai thane vachen
needu doshamantatikai, rakthamu kaarchenu
shikshanu pondenu, sriyesun cherumu “Randi”
5. Paapularaa parugidirandi paapula mitrudesuni cherudi
shaktito ninnu rakshinchunu santosamichunu
sandehapadaku, suvarthan nammumu “Randi”
6. Needu papamu nantatini neevu nikkamuga noppukonina
ayane tanaraktamuto, kadugu premato
kaapaadu nerputho, karuna sakthitho “Randi”


. 341.Iruku margambulo pravesinchu || ఇరుకు మార్గంబులో ప్రవేశించు
Mathew - 7:13
Tang darwaze ho kar
Pallavi : Iruku margambulo pravesinchu varu kondare
Yesu raktambuna shuddiyagu vaaru kondare
1. Yellaru ee loka soukhyamunu pondajuturu
kondare sramalayandu paalu goredu vaaru “Eruku”
2. Saitaanutho poraadi jayamu nonda gorina
somyuktudavu kavalenu prabhu yesunito “Eruku”
3. Paduchesitivi dhustatwambulo nee jeevitamu
nedaina nee paapamulanundi vidudalondedavaa “Eruku”
4. Yesu sevakai nee jevitamu narpinchumu
Yesuku nee pranamu nichunanta preminchumu“Eruku”


. 342.Krupa kalamu dati povuchunnadi || కృపకాలము దాటిపోవుచున్నది
2cornthi - 6:2
Krupa kalamu dati povuchunnadi
Pallavi : Krupakaalamu daatipovuchunnadi
krupapondanu parugidi randu vevega
1. Pagalu daatipoyenu - raatri vachchu chunnadi
digululeka Yesuni sontamugaa cherudi “Krupa”
2. Paapa aasha veeduchu, lokamaitri veeduchu
paapamannimpondiye jeeva maargamu cheru “Krupa”
3. Sontha kriyalu mundunu venuka nandhakaaramu
nanthamagni kolomiye itti maargamanduna “Krupa”
4. Repu needi yagunaa marana vela theliyunaa ?
praapakudu Yesudu vachu vela theeliyunaa ? “Krupa”
5. Antya kristu vachunu narula mosaginchunu
antha paapa madhikamai deva bhakti thaggunu “Krupa”
6. Donga bhakhti veeduchu boothu bhaasha viduchuchu
dandanaku thappumu shiksha raakamundugaa “Krupa”
7. Enni maarlu rakshana vaartha viniyu nammaka
yunnavaaru krupakai lechi angalaarturu “Krupa”
8. Vyaadhi shramalu maranamo veru etti kastamo
baadhinchaka mundugaa nesunodda karugumu “Krupa”
9. Ninnu prabhuvu throyaka narakamunaku pampaka
yundunatlu daiva krupa ponda yesunu cheru “Krupa”
10. Aadi prema bhrastulai allalaadi jeevinchu
maanavulanu choodaka Yesu vibhuni choodumaa “Krupa”


. 343.Prabhu Yesuke jayamanipaadu || ప్రభు యేసుకే జయమని పాడు

chakkani maargamu joopenu
inkanu niluvaku paapamulo “Prabhu”

yesu ninu vidipinchunu

. 344.Caluvarilo vimukhti - kaligeno priyundaa || కలువరిలో విముక్తి - కలిగెనో ప్రియుండా

2. Paada hastamula nundi - prakka gaayamu nundi pravahinchenu punya - pranayaamrutha dhaara “Caluvari”
3. Prabhu Yesuni rakhtame - premaamrutha dhaara priyamaaraga thraagu - prabhusannidhijeri “Caluvari”
4. Ghana premanu joopi - thana rakhtamucheta thaane kadugunu - mana paapamu nantha “Caluvari”

paapulanu rakshinchu - praadehata nimmu “Caluvari”


. 345.Yesu prabhuve gaaka vasudhalo || యేసు ప్రభువేగాక - వసుధలో

paraloka midina paddathi gaadu “Yesu”

thwarapadi satyamu jerumunedu “Yesu”
5. Yesuku nenu nivaasamu kaagaa
sustira maayenu naa rakshana “Yesu”

. 346.Prabhu sriyesu - prabhu sri yesu || ప్రభు శ్రీ యేసు

. 347.Paripurnambagu guruvu yevaru  || పరిపూర్ణంబగు గురువు యెవరు

2. Ihamunu vidichina tyagiye gada - mahaasatya sadguruvu
kapatamu daaguleni subuddhi - karunamaya hrudayudu “Pari”

premananda samaadhaanamutho-poorthiga nimpunu manalan “Pari”

tanapai mana papumulanu mosi -

. 348.Prajalara vegame raare || ప్రజలారా వేగమే రారే

yemaina bedamuleka - Yesayya brochunu vega “Praja”
3. Papatmule thanasutulu - prabhu yesuniki snehitulu
nee papamella boyen - neekinka mokshamu kalugun “Praja”
4. Prayasapadi baramunu - mosedi O prajalara
prabhu Yesu kristu meeku - prashaanthi nitchunu randi “Praja”

doshambulellanu bapi - aashirvadinchunu gaachi “Praja”


. 349.Premamrutha dhaarala chindina mana || ప్రేమామృత ధారల చిందిన మన

. 351.Randi randi yesuni yoddaku || రండి రండి యేసుని యొద్దకు

. 352.Rarandi yesu padamula chera || రారండి యేసు పాదముల చేర

. 356.Maanava roopamunu dharinchi  || మానవ రూపమును ధరించి

Yesunu sweekarinchumu nee swantha rakshakunigaa

. 357.Saatilenidi Yesuni rakhtamu || సాటి లేనిది యేసుని రక్తము
I John - 1:7
Yishu ka lohu anupam hai jo
Pallavi : Saatilenidi Yesuni rakhtamu paapamunu
kadugunu priyudaa paapamunu
kadugunu
1. Choodumu sodaraa devudu entho - preminche
ee jagatin priyudaa preminche ee jagatin - siluvalo
praanamu narpincha kristu Yesuni pampenu -
priyudaa Yesuni pampenu “Saati”
2. Lokamuna karudenchi kristu prabhuvu - praanamu
baligaanitche priyudaa praanamu baligaanitche -
lokapaapamella siluvalo mosi tholaginche shaapamunpriyudaa
tholaginche shaapamun “Saati”
3. Vinumu sodaraa prabhu Yesu kristuni - paraloka
vaartanu priyudaa paraloka vaartanu - unnathamaina
paraloka premanu chaatinchu chuntimi -
priyudaa chaatinchu chuntimi “Saati”
4. Yesuni neevu kshaminchumani vedu - virigina
hrudayamutho priyudaa virigina hrudayamutho -
Yesuni amoolya rakhta dhaarale kadugunu paapamellapriyudaa
kadugunu paapamella “Saati”
5. Paapa bhaaramunu mosikoni neevu - prayaasa
mondedavaa ? Priyudaa prayaasa mondedavaa ? paapamoppukoni Yesu paadamula chentaku jerumu- priyudaa chentaku jerumu “Saati”
6. Gatinchu chunnadi swalpa jeevitamu - sheegrahmugaa rammu priyudaa sheegrahmugaa rammu - kartha Yesu nandu viswaasamunchi rakshana
pondumu - priyudaa rakshana pondumu “Saati”
7. Krupayaanandamu pavitra premalo - bhaagamu pondumu - priyudaa bhaagamu pondumu - paapa saagaramunu daatincha galadu Yesu rakshakudepriyudaa
Yesu rakshakude “Saati”


. 358.Rakshana nosagedu Yesuni || రక్షణ నొసగెడు యేసుని
Isiah - 55:6

Pallavi : Rakshana nosagedu Yesuni premanu lakshyamu cheyumu o priyudaa akshaya raajyamu neeyanu vachina - rakshakun bogadumu snehithudaa
1. Lokapu premanu yemani thelpeda - nee kavamaanambe dalachinacho maarani Yesuni rakshakun prema - dhaakudu nondumu o priyudaa “Rakshana”
2. Paapapu premalo viduvaka nilichina - thaapamu chendeda vo narudaa paapini gaavanu prema swaroopudu - shaapamu norchenu calvarilo “Rakshana”
3. Chachchina paapini vedaki rakshimpa - chachchi brathikina ghanu devadu vachina paapini vaddani throyani - nishchala premaa mayudu Yese “Rakshana”
4. Nammumu sodaraa ninnu rakshinchunu - nemmadi
nondedavu nijamu namminacho prabhu premanu gaanavu - nammumu prabhu prema neediname “Rakshana”
5. Ghana dhani kula matha soundharyambulan - gaanavu nija premaa dharanal ennila nunnanu niluchune nityamu - pennuga pondumu prabhu preman “Rakshana”
6. Tandri kumaara shuddatmala chittamun - dandiga neraverchuchu ghanulu endaro negiri pondanu
makutamu - pondumu prabhu prema - Halleluya “Rakshana”


. 359.Papulakoraku prabhuyesu || పాపులకొరకు ప్రభుయేసు

. 360.Devudu lokamunu yentho preminchenu || దేవుడు లోకమును యెంతో ప్రేమించెను

. 361.Maya lokamu - mosapokumu  || మాయ లోకము - మోసపోకుము

. 377.Yesuni venta nenu - vembadinchuchunnanu || యేసుని వెంట నేను - వెంబడించుచున్నాను

“Thana”


. 378.Neevennallu rendu thalampulatho || నీవెన్నాళ్ళు రెండు తలంపులతో
Pallavi : Neevennallu rendu thalampulatho –
kunti kunti nadicheda veevu
Yehovaye nee devuda? Leka vere devathalunnara?
1. Manam thermaninchedamipude – mananota vanchana lekunda
Marugaina papamulanniti – Hrudayamunundi tholaginchedam
2. Maru manassu pondedamipude – jeevithamosamulanundi
Parisuddalamai nirdoshuluga – prabhudinamandu kanapadedam
3. Apavadiki chotivvaka – bahujagratthatho nundedamu
Manushyulanu santhoshapettaka – daiva chittamulo nilichedamu
4. Nenu na inti varalamu – yehovane sevinchedamu
Neevevarini sevinchedavo – ee diname theermaninchuko
5. Padipoyina Nee balipeetamun – saricheyutaku neevu siddama
Israelu devuni vedina – agni moolamuga badulitchunu
6. Intha varaku ninnu nadipina – Ebinejaraina nee devuni
Neevu marachi jeevinchinacho – neeku nemmadiye undadu
7. Dvandva jeevitha margamulu – yeruguduva asthiramulani
Poornamanassutho prabhunvedakina – poorna mahimatho nindedavu


. 379.Painunna aakasamanduna  || పైనున్న ఆకాశమందునా

Ledu papa vimochana aa - aa - (2) “Painunna”

Yesu namame - rakshana margam “Painunna”

. 380.Yesu prabhuve lokarakshakudu  || యేసు ప్రభువే లోకరక్షకుడు

. 385.Vinathi vinathi vinathi triyekuniki  || వినతి వినతి వినతి త్రియేకునికి

. 387.Prabhu Yesu pilupunu || ప్రభు యేసు పిలుపును
2 Corinth - 6:2
Prabhu Yesu pilupunu
Pallavi : Prabhu Yesu pilupunu O priyudaa pedachevini pettedavaa - theermaanamu cheyakane velledavaa- prabhu sannidhilo nundi
1. Letha vayassu nadipraayamunu - gathinchi povunavi mannayinadi venukativalene - marala bhoomiki,cherun aatma daani dayachesina - devuni yoddaku povun aa lokamulo nee mundu gathi emouno erigithivaa “Prabhu”
2. Epaatidi nee jeevitha mantha - epaatidi nee thanuvu gaddi puvvutho samamidi yera - adiye nee jeevitamu
antalona maayamu agu - vintha budagaye kadaa antalona anthardhanambagu aaviri ye kadaa “Prabhu”
3. Vyardhamu vyardhamu sarvamu ilalo - idiye Yesuni maata niluvani needa ee lokomuraa - kalushaathma kanugonaraa lokamantha sampaadinchi - lobhee nee praanamunu nasta parachu konina neeku narudaa laabhamu kaladaa “Prabhu”
4. Thaamasincha thagadika neeku - thakshaname thirugumuraa virigi naligi hrudayamu kaligi - vinayamutho prabhu jeri yesu prabhuni siluva chenta - Yesuni rakhtamu kori pralaapinchi needu sakala paapamu noppukonumaa “Prabhu”
5. Nee rakshanakai nilichenu Yesu - thana rakhta dhaaralatho
kadugunu ninnu kshamiyinchunu - vadigaa ee kshanamande nee naamamunu paralokamulo - nede vraasi yunchun
rakshanaanandamutho nippude ranjilledavu priyudaa “Prabhu”


. 388.Prematho yesu - piluchuchunnaadu  || ప్రేమతో యేసు - పిలుచుచున్నాడు

kaapari swarmau dwaninche - parugidirammu “Prema”

krupa kaalamide jaagela - parugidi rammu “Prema”

. 394.Yesu prabhuve neeku rakshana  || యేసు ప్రభువే - నీకు రక్షణ
Heb - 2:4
"Intha goppa rakshanu manamu nirlakshyamu chesinayedala
elaagu thappinchu kondumu"
Yishu Prabhu hai tera Taranhara
Pallavi : Yesu prabhuve neeku rakshana nitchunu
intha goppa rakshana nirlakshya pettaku “Yesu”
1. Mruthiye paapapu jeetamu - prabhuni varamu jeevamu
kristu nangeekarinchina nitya jeeva mitchchunu
praanamun aasiluvapaini baligaa nidi nin konegadaa
maruthuvaa Yesuni premanu - maruvaku “Yesu”
2. Kantiki kanabadani venno - cheviki vinabadavi nenno
grahimpa shakyamu kaanivi - neekai sidda parachenu
praanamun aa siluvapaini - baligaa nidi nin konegadaa
pedachevin pettaku yesuni - maatanu “Yesu”
3. Marana balamu gala vaanin - naashanamubu chesenu
marana bhayamu lonunna - vaarini vidipinchenu
praanamun aa siluva paini - baligaa nidi nin kone
gadaa Hrudayamun teruvumu Yesunu - cherchuko “Yesu”
4. Siluva rakhtamu chetanu - nirdhevu laina vaarini
madyapu godanu padagotti - aikyaparache devunitho
praanamun aa siluvapaini - baligaa nidi nin konegadaa
Samadhana padu mika devunito - eekshaname “Yesu”
5. Daiva swabhaavambulo - parishuddaatmuni yandu
paralokapu pilupulo - paali vaarala jesenu
praanamun aa siluva paini - baligaa nidi nin konegadaa
parishuddula swaastyamulo paali bhaga mondum “Yesu”
6. Devuni parishuddatalo - kaluga bovu mahimalo
kristu Yesu prabhuvulo - paalivaarala jesenu
praanamun aa siluva paini baligaa nidi nin konegadaa
thwara padu needu bhaagamu pondanu “Yesu”
7. Paralokamulo kanabadu thellanaina vastramul
dharinchukonu samoohamu - kharjooru mattalu chebooni
devunikini gorrepillakunu - stotramulu cheyuchunda
neevu nee rakshana kai paadumu Halleluya “Yesu”


. 395.Oh paapi sandhinchitivaa || ఓపాపీ - సంధించితివా

nee praanamunaku shaanthi nosagun
1. Baadhimpa bade prabhu Yesu - vidudala jeya ninnu nindanu pondenu - ponda nee vaanandam “O paapi”
2. Kristu yesu nee korakedche - getsamane vanamulo vaatsalyamutho - ninnaanandimpa jeyun “O paapi”
3. Rakshakudu theerpukai - niliche akshaya jeeva meeya sikshanu bonde - ninnaandimpa jeya “O paapi”
4. Prabhuvaina Yesu thattuchunnaadu - nee hrudaya dwaaramun abbunu shaanthi - therachina hrudayamun “O paapi”
5. Jeeva jala mitchu prabhuvaina Yesu - dappigoni yunna neeku jeevithaanthamu varaku - dappigona ne maatramu “O paapi”
6. Rakshana durgamuna ninnunchi - shatruvunu anachivesi dakshina hastamutho - kappunu - ninnepudu “O paapi”
7. Devuni swaramu - vinudi nede - daivaputru louduru
sevinchudi kristuni jeevitamularpinchi “O paapi”


. 396.Choodumu sodarudaa neevu || చూడుము సోదరుడా నీవు
John 1:4
Choodumu sodarudaa
Pallavi : Choodumu sodarudaa neevu - nede lechi rakshana korakai
vedumu snehithudaa

lechi raa nammumu sodarudaa “Choodumu”
2. Devuni vaakyamu velugai yunnadi -
aa veluge neeku jeevamai yunnadi
nee venuke aajeevamu nilachenu - jeevamu nondaga vegame raa
raavo sodarudaa “Choodumu”
3. Niluvumu nee jeevamu aaviriye -
ilalo ledika needani cheppedu
kalushamu lellanu kadugunu kristu niluchunu ila nee kaapariyai
caluvari chentaku raa “Choodumu”
4. Morra pettumu nede lechi - sarichesukoni jeevitha mantha
parishudda rakhta dhaaralatho - parishuddudu nilachenu neekai
parugidi raa priyudaa “Choodumu”
5. Yesuni nammedi vaarilalona - Yesuni jeevam pondina vaarai
bhaasurambugaa moksham jera - nilchedaru shakhtini bondi
Yese osagunu raa “Choodumu”
6. Halleluya paadumu neede - vallabhundu Yesu vachchunani
ella prajalu choocheda resun - challani prabhu raaka ilalo
stutulanu paadanu raa “Choodumu”


. 397.Prabhu thattu kannuleththu || ప్రభుతట్టు కన్ను లెత్తు

. 398.Choodumu neevu melconumu  || చూడుము నీవు మేలుకొనుము

. 399.Yesuni sweekarinchu || యేసుని స్వీకరించు

Paluvidhamulagu vedhigrstulkuswasthatha
nechchru taskshnume

. 400.Jeevitha mevvariki nee jeevitha mevvariki || జీవిత మెవ్వరికి, నీ జీవిత మెవ్వరికి

Pallavi : Jeevitha mevvariki nee jeevitha mevvariki ?
ee lokomulo jeevinchu jeevithamantha
jeevitha mevvariki nee jeevitha mevvariki ?
1. Shareerechalapai aashalundu - ee dharani yandu
sukhabhogulugaa jeevinturu - ee dharani yandu
vaari yoohalu dinamella chediyunnavi
vaari paapa jeevitha mantha shaapamega
2. Dhanapeksu lendaro galaru - ee dharani yandu
dhanamupai manassu nilpedaru - ee dharani yandu
vaari kalavara mantha dhanamu dhaname
vaaru brathikedu brathukantha kshanathaye
3. Swantha bodhalakai brathikedaru - ee dharani yandu
garvamunaku ammabadi yunduru - ee dharani yandu
vaari manasulu sankuchitamulai yundu
vaari jeevitha prayaasamu - pathanamegaa
4. Virigina hrudayamulu kalarendaro - ee dharani yandu
karigedu uppuga nundedaru - ee dharani yandu
vaaru prabhukai daagiye nilachedaru
daiva vaakkuga dinamella sevinturu

. 406.Prabhu yesu rammanuchunde || ప్రభుయేసు రమ్మనుచుండె

. 407.Yerushalemu gummamulaara rajunu || యెరుషలేము గుమ్మములారా రాజును

. 408.Theruvu nee hrudaya dwarambu nede || తెరువు నీ హృదయ ద్వారంబు నేడే

. 409.Krupakaalamulo prabhuyesune || కృపకాలములో - ప్రభుయేసుని

. 411.Teruvabadi yunnadi krupadwaramu || తెరువబడియున్నది కృపద్వారము

. 413.Daari tholagitivela || దారితొలగితివేల

. 414.Lokamunu vidachi vellavalenuga  || లోకమును విడచి వెళ్ళవలెనుగ

Pallavi : Lokamunu vidachi vellavalenuga
sarva michatane viduva valen
1. Yaatrikulamu ee dustalokamulo - paadulokamulo
mana kedi ledu - ye vishaya mandaina
garvinchalemu - jaagrathagane nadachu konedamu “Loka”
2. Kasta baadhalache brathu kantha ninde - kanneellu
niraasha nispruhala mayamu - karunaa kataakshamu
nammedamu - kristu prabhunipai drusti nunchedamu “Loka”
3. Entha varaku ee bhuvi yandudedamo - saitaanutho
sadaa poraatamegaa - shatruni thanthraala
nergitimi - dhairyamuthone kona saagedamu “Loka”
4. Gatamu nanthatini marachi poyedamu - guri yodda
kaanandamutho velledamu - maargaana vacheti
shramala norchi - arhula moudamu bahumaanamonda “Loka”
5. Mana eershya kapata dweshaalu vidachi - nija prema -
thone jeevinchedamu - nishkalankulamai shuddulamai -
pari poornathanu che pattudamu “Loka”
6. Jeevamu gala prabhu rakshinche manala - vimochinchi
nootana jeevamosage - koni pova kristu thwaragaa
vachun - anduche manamu siddapadedamu “Loka”
7. Aatmeeya netraalatho choochedamu - entha adbuthamu
soundharya nagaram - prabhuvu chentaku velledamu -
vijayotsavamutho praveshinchedamu “Loka”


. 415.Nee jeevitamulo gamyambu yedo || నీ జీవితములో - గమ్యంబుయేదో

. 419.Peda naruni rupamu dharinchi || పేద నరుని రూపము దరించి
Pallavi : Peda naruni rupamu dharinchi
Yesu raadu nee chenta nilache
Angikarinchu mayananu

Mullamakutamu sirassuna pettabade
Ninda veedana sramalanu sahinche nesu

Deenudai ninnu piluchuchunde “Peda”
2. Thalavalchutaku ila sthalameledu
Dappi theerchukona neeru dorakaledu
Thannu aadarinchu varevaru leru
Priya rakshakudu siluvalo vrelade
Patlupade ninnu vidipimpanu “Peda”
3. Prabhu sathanu thalanu chituka drokken
Papadagulan rakthamutho kadigen
Nee vyadhini vedana tholagincha
Nee sapamunundi vidipimpa
Siluvalo vijayamu ponde “Peda”
4. Mayalokamunu neevu nammakumu
Manushyula manassu maripovu nila
Nityadevuni premanu nammineevu
Nischayamuga prabhuvulo anandimpa
Neud rammu viswasamutho “Peda”
5. Thamasincheda vela O priyuda
Priya yesuni yoddaku lechirammu
Ee lokamu neekivvani santhini
Ee diname prabhuvu neekosaga
Prematho ninnu pilachuchunde “Peda”


. 420.Naadu hrudayapu dwaaram || నాదు హృదయపు ద్వారము

. 436.Dayagala Yesu paapi kaashrayudaa || దయగలయేసు పాపికాశ్రయుడా

Ee naade nannu kshaminchumu
naa peru grandhamandu vraayumu “Daya”


. 437.Sangha mokkate, saarvathrika  || సంఘమొక్కటే, సార్వత్రిక
CHURCH - SANGHAMU
John-17:21
Mandali ek hi hai
Pallavi : Sangha mokkate, saarvathrika sanghamanedi sangha mokkate
A.P. : Shirassu nokate shareera mokate - nitya shakhti galginatti
1. Ye naruni peruleni sanghamidi - yesiddaanthapu peruleni sanghamu - staana dinamula peru lenididi - elaati peru vahinchani yatti “Sangha”
2. Yoodulani helleneyulani ledu - sunnathi pondiyunna lekunnanu - desheeyudu paradeshee yani ledu - swaatantrya daasya stree purushudanleni “Sangha”
3. Aatmaikyamanu yedu petala thraadu - ee thraatiche sanghamu katta badenu - itti jeevamu kalgi lokamunaku - veraina jeevamu jeevinchuchunnatti “Sangha”
4. Sanghame shareeram shareerame sangham - divya
drustaanthamulatho nindinadi devuni illaayana
nivaasa stalam - naveena varudu raaja nagaramu illu “Sangha”
5. Intiki punaadhi aadhaara mainatlu - draakshavallilo
theegelu nilchunatlu - nara shareramunaku
thalavale - bhaaryaku bharthavale kristunugala “Sangha”
6. Saarvathrika sabhanu kaanagaleni - kaaranaana saitaanu
kalavaramu nonde - stala sanghamu dwaara -
saarvathrika maina - sanghamunu joopa veelagu nijamu “Sangha”
7. Maru janma mondina vaare ee sanghamu - asamaanu
desude yaddaani shiramu - yogyamugaa naidu sevala
jethumu - mudamuna paadumu - yesuku Halleluya “Sangha”


. 438.Parishuddha shriyesuve - paralokaraaju || పరిశుద్ధ శ్రీ యేసువే - పరలోకరాజు
Daniel 4:26
Parishuddha Sri Yesuve
Pallavi : Parishuddha shriyesuve - paralokaraaju
muriyuchu ne poojinthunu - nirathamu
A. P. : Paraloka mahimanundi - narula raajyamulalo nirathamu
thana paalanamu jariginchu chunna raaju
1. Penuyelu poraatambuna - ponivvananchu
penugunanduna Yaakobu - vinayamuna
nannu deevinchu thandri - ninnu ne viduvananchu
kanneetitho vedagaa - ghanatha israayelaniye “Pari”
2. Ee dinamuna nundi - padilamuga
mudamuga deevinthunanen - aadarana kartha
thudimandira punaadipai - kadalaka niluchuvaarin
kadalani naa punaadi - yoodaa gothra simhambu “Pari”
3. Sionulonundi - priyudaina Yesu
kaayuchu ninu deevinchunu - aayana throvan
paayaka ninnepudu - paripaalinchu chundunu
rayamuna ninnu jeri - saayambu cheyu chundun “Pari”
4. Jayinchu chunna vaaniki - marugaina mannaa
priyamuna bhajiyimpanitchun - jayashaali
vraayabadina krotha naamamunnatti thella raayi
nosangi vaani bhayamu tholaginchu jayamu “Pari”
5. Nadipinchu chundi nityamu - thana drushti nilipi
viduvakundaga nee prabhu - kadavaraku edathegani
thanadu prema - kanu parachi thruptiparachi
chedugunellanu baapi - thana yadugu jaadalalo “Pari”
6. Balamu naaropinchumu - balamitchu prabhuvu
siluvalo neekai samasenu - sionu geliche
samaadhinundi - balamutho thirigi leche
ella melula thalachi - Halleluya paadedamu “Pari”


. 439.Jayinchuvadu Deva kumarudu || జయించువాడు దేవకుమారుడు
Rev. 21:7
jayinchuvadu Deva kumarudu
1. Jayinchuvaadu devakumaarudu - bhayamu
chendaka yundudi sarvamu pogottaka

2. Adi prema vidina Ephes sanghamaa - adiye nee
koratha jayinchina neevu jeeva phalamulanu -
priyamuga bhujiyinthuvu
3. Shrestathamagu Smurnaa sanghamaa shramalanu
ne maruvan - jayinchina neeku rendava maranamu
bhayapadi haani cheyadu
4. Pergamu sabha nee bodhayu, thappudu - maargamula
nerugudun - jayinchina marugaina mannaa
krotha peru thellani raatinithun
5. Thuyathaira sabha nee shakhti nerugudun -
neebhayamula nerugudun jayinchina janulapai
nadhikaara mithun - vekuva chukka nithun
6. Saardis sabha nee chaavu ne nerugudu - thwaralona
stirapadumu - jayinchina neeku thellani vastramu -
lichi ninnoppu kondunu
7. Priyamagu oh Philadelphia sanghamaa - nee
aashakyatha theliyun - jayinchina stambhamugaa
nunchi neeku - kroththa naamamu nidudun
8. Lavodikeya sabha nee lakshanamula - daurbhagyatha
theliyun jayinchina ninnu simhaasanamuna -
naatho koorchunda nithun
9. Jayamondu vidhamunu thelpiti nindu - jayinchu
vaari bhaagyamu apajayamunu pondu vidhamuna
delpiti - neevetu nilchedavo


. 440.Siyonu pattanamaa || సీయోనుపట్టణమా
zechar- 9:9
He Syyon nagar tu sone ka nagar hai
1. Siyonu pattanamaa - suvarna nagaramaa - mahimaapuramaa
mahaa bhaagyamu neede - ramya mainatti
raa raaju puramaa
2. Siyonu sundarulu - suvarna samulu - vanne
pagadaala chchaaya kanna goppadi -
kaanthi neelamula kanna manchidi
3. Prabhuve ninnu kori preminchinaadu -
sarvonnathude ninnu stiramu jesenu -
nitya nivaasamuga ninuu jesenu
4. Thana chanti pillanu thalli marachunaa -
marachina gaani nenu maruvanu ninnu -
chekkitini ninu naa yara chetula meeda
5. Bhaya mela siyonu - bala mondi lemmu
santasamuna paata saahaasamuna paadudi
vasiyinchu nee prabhuvu vachchi neelo
6. Pendli kumaarudu - pendli koothurunu
choochu natlu ninnu - choochi devudu siyonu
nee yandu santasa mondun
7. Siyonu paga vaaru siggu nondedaru - ninnu
baadhinchi natti nee paga vaaru paruguna
nee paadamulapai badedaru
8. Siyonu nee neethi soorya kaanthi vale

veliginchu varaku vishraminchadu


. 441.Siyonu puramaa - sarvonnathuni || సీయోను పురమా - సర్వోన్నతుని

. 442.Prabhu yesu sanghamu nirminchu || ప్రభుయేసు సంఘము నిర్మించుచుండ

7. Prakatinchedamu praakatamu ganu

pogaduchu shirassunu paadeda mipude “Prabhu”

. 444.Santasillunu mee hrudayaalu || సంతసిల్లును మీ హృదయాలు

. 445.Shakhtigala shaalemu raajaa || శక్తిగల షాలేమురాజా షారోను రోజా
Mathew 16:18
Shaktishali, Raja Shalem ka, Gulab

stutiyinchedamu Yesu
1. Poorvamuna palkina nee pravachanokhtulanni chakkaganu
makkuvatho chesitivi neevu - chesitivi neevupoorvamuna
choopina nee pratyakshata lanni - varusaganu jaripitivi
ninnu polinavaadu verevvaru leru “Shaktigala”
2. Bayalu parachinatti namoonaanu poli naadu balamuganu
needu pratyaksha gudaaramunu - nee gudaaramunu
kattitivi nee daasudai natti Moshe dwaraa nimpitivi
nindaina nee prabhaava mahimanu - prabhaava mahimanu
“Shaktigala”
3. Shaalemu yerushalemuloni aalayamu Solomonu dwaraa
kattinchina maharaajaa - kattinchina raajaa aalayamunu
nirminchinatti maharaajaa nimpitivi nindaina nee
prabhaava mahimanu prabhaava mahimanu “Shaktigala”
4. Kaalamu sampoornamuga parinaminchagane kanya garbamuna

naa sanghamu nani selavitchi kattuchunnaavu mammula
nee swaroopamunaku - nee aalayamuganu “Shaktigala”
5. Hasta kruthaalayamulo vasinchani neevu vintagaanu
maa madyanu unda gori naavu - undagori naavu - kaanti -
vantamaina needu mahaa mahimathone swanta vaarinantha
nimpa theermaaninchi naavu - theermaaninchinaavu
“Shaktigala”
6. Akkadanu ikkada nokkokkarini yeri adbuthamuganu
jatha cheyu vaada veevu - cheyuvaada veevu - noothana
dampatulanu vintagaa deevinchi antakantaku vardhilla
jeyuvaada veeve - kaayuvaada veeve “Shaktigala”
7. Vyakhtulanu kutumbamulanugaa maarchivesi shakhtigala
sangha vadhuvuga maarchivesi - neeve maarchivesi
vintagaa naa vadhuvunaku varundavai naavu antamu
ledahaa nee mahima raajyamunaku - Halleluya amen
“Shaktigala”


. 446.Daiva darshanamuna Yaakobu || దైవదర్శనమున యాకోబు

. 452.Prabhu dayacheyu nitya || ప్రభు దయచేయు - నిత్య

shakhti heenulamaipoyi nappudu

nijamugaa chooturu “Prabhu”
3. Prabhu yuddamu cheyu naayakudu
prabhu pakshamandu cherumu
eenaade - neevu pondedavu
Berakaalo nijamugaa jayamu “Prabhu”
4. Paluvidha shramalandu cherumaa
preeti meera mimmu daricherchunu
neethi yukhtamugaa stutinchumu
khyaatitho prabhuni “Prabhu”
5. Nitya devuni mahaa krupa
niratam shatruvunu jayinchunu
nishchayam - kruthajnathaa stutulu
meeru nityamugaa chellinchudi “Prabhu”
6. Swaramandala sitaaraa vayinchudi
shatruvulatho prabhu porusalpenu
Berakaalo prabhu swarameththi
mari mari paadudi “Prabhu”
7. Parama thandri prasaadinchu
nemmadi - bhooraajulu gada gada
vanikiri - thana prajalanu santhosha
paruchunu - Halleluya paadudi “Prabhu”


. 453.Nirmimpabaditimi manamu || నిర్మింపబడితిమి మనము దైవగృహముగా

. 454.Stutinchumu stutinchumu  || స్తుతించుము స్తుతించుము

meppudu - stutiki yogyudu - mana prabhuve

badithimi - Yesu prabhuni naipunya hastamu
nirminche nillu - poornamugaa

. 458.Maname prabhuni paraloka gruhamu || మనమే ప్రభుని పరలోక గృహము

. 469.Devuni mahima mandiram || దేవుని మహిమ మందిరం

8. Munupati mahimanu minchina mahimatho
Paralokamu nundi digi vatchuchunna
Noothana yerooshalemade “Devuni”

. 472.Kristuni swaramu vindunu prabhuve || క్రీస్తుని స్వరము విందును ప్రభువే

. 481.Nee swaramu vinupinchu prabhuvaa  || నీ స్వరము వినిపించు ప్రభువా

. 485.Nadrsti nipai nilipi || నా దృష్టి నీపై నిలిపి

nilucunu nilakadaga yadarthula mora yehova vinulu vinunu vidaka sahanamuto || Na drusti ||

santosincunu bahu menduganu mahimalo vesenu vinayamuga
mandira punadini mugincunatani cetulu mudamuna jarugunidi daivatmace || Na drusti ||
3. Daivasana peddala madhya campinatlunna sajiva gottepilla
yesuni kannulu ninnu kanaga jivincucunnananu koninan
mrtudave nivilalo davanaiyunna vatini sarididdu jagratta yesuni svaramu vinu || Na drusti ||
4. Madilo parama prabhuvunerugu - yadardha hrdayula balaparaca
prdivi lo payaninci cūdaga prabhudrsti yehovanu vidi vellenu asa - siriya raju dariki
mati tappi nivu madi vartincitivi - idi modalu niku yud'dhamule || Na drusti ||
5. Svardhamuto nenabaddinai - vyardhamuga nadicina yedala
mosamukai tvarapadi - na padamu parugidina
drstincu prabhu natrovalanu lekkincu adugulanu
devuderugu na yadardhatantayu - tarici tūcunu trasulo || Na drusti ||
6. Edu atmala upadesam - edu saṅghamulu heccarinca
rūdhiga meghamuna prabhu vegamilaku raga
bitito gancu prati netram - podicina varu saha
lokulu rom'munu badukonduru - bahu sid'dhama nivu prabhuni cera || Na drusti ||
7. Prabhu alocana nilucu sada prabhusaṅkalpamu tara taramul
sanstutito nitiparulu kristu sannidhani anandincudi devunilo
ksitini prati ksanamu yadardha hrdayulandaru
ekamai ceyudi ullasa ganamu || Na drusti ||

“Yesuni”


. 487.Yehovaanu stutinchudi - aayana || యెహోవాను స్తుతించుడి

. 492.Devudu meeku ellappudu thoduga || దేవుడు మీకు ఎల్లప్పుడు

. 493.Ellappudu ellappudu ellappudu || ఎల్లప్పుడు ఎల్లప్పుడు ఎల్లప్పుడు

. 497.Parishuddulai yundudi daiva || పరిశుద్ధులై యుండుడి

. 498.Premaa premaa - premaa || ప్రేమా ప్రేమా - ప్రేమా

. 499.Erigiyuntive - Yehovaa || ఎరిగియుంటివే - యెహోవా

nirdevudanai nenundagane - neetiga tirchitive

Yesukristunandu nannu - mahima
tejomayamuga diviraajyamuna -
doota - ganambulu pritiga pogada
tarugani nityatandri mahimatomahima
rupudagu mariya sutunito - mahima parachitive

. 503.Nene bhayapadakudadanenu || నేనే భయపడ కూడదనెను

. 504.Manamu Yesu prabhuni mahima || మనము యేసు ప్రభుని మహిమ

2. Neevu nammina yedala - devuni mahima chutuvu
jeeva punaruddhanamu Yesu
3. Pratyakshagudaramunu - meghamu kammagane
Yehova thejassu nindenu
4. Devuni nivaasamu - manujulatho nunnadi
nivasinchu - devude vaarilo
5. Mahima prabavamuto - makutamu darinchina kristu
thanayulanu thechche mahimaku
6. Mana rakshana kartanu shramato - sampoornuni jeya
mana tandrike thagiyunnadi
7. Mana chulakani shramalu - raabovu mahima yeduta ennataginavi kaavu
8. Parishudda pattanamulo - devunike mahima
prabhuvunake mahima halleluya


. 505.Devaa ! nee thalampulu naa || దేవా! నీ తలంపులు నా
Psalm-139:17
He Ishwar Tere vichar
Pallavi : Devaa ! nee thalampulu naa kentho priyamu - entho priyamu - vaati moththamu daasuda nagu ne nenchi cheppeda goppadi goppadi
1. Paataalapu paashamulu - nannu arikattagaa - aavarinche marana urulu - krungi potino devaa - krungi potino devaa praardhanalo morrapetta - vinitvi naa deena dwani anduke ne paadeda - keertincheda “Devaa”
2. Naa meediki lechuvaaru - nannu bedarincheduvaaru devaa
nee rakshana naa nundi daati poyenane vaaru - daatipoye nane vaaru - praardhanalo morrapetta - vinitivi na deena dwani anduke ne paadeda - keertincheda “Devaa”
3. Neeve naa kaapari nantivi - kaapu dalalo raaleka yuntini paapinai yundi paapa merugananti shaapa grastuda naiti devaa praardhanalo morrapetta - vinitivi naa deena dwani anduke - ne paadeda - keertincheda “Deeva”
4. Mootha vesina naa morkhathayunu - daagi yundina naa paapamunu vippi choopi shikshimpa nantivi - kaksha leni naa devaa - Kakshaleni naa deva arhatha leni vaadanu -
sarvamu poyina vaadanu anduke ne - paadeda keertincheda “Devaa”
5. Nenu nee kattadalanu - nerchukonu natlunu shrama pondi yunduta naaku melani nerpinchitivi - melani nerpinchitivi - nee dharma shaastramu naaku priyamu - dina mella nenu dyaaninthunu anduke ne paadeda - keertincheda “Devaa”
6. Parvathamulu tholagi poyinanu - thatharillina mettalu mattamai ottu pettukoni nenu cheppeda vidichipodu nin naadu krupa vidichipodu nin naadu krupa - nee vaakhdaanamulakenaa stotramu naa aartha dwanulu naa hrudaya dhyaanam - angeekarinchu devaa - keertincheda “Devaa”
7. Nenu cheyunadi ipudu - neevu eruga jaalavane thelisikonduvu neevu ika munduku - naa paripoorna maargamide - naa paripoorna maarga mide - vintini ne nee swaramu - kantinine
nee roopamu - Halleluya paadeda - keertincheda “Devaa”

Pallavi : Sarvamulo sarvadaa - Yesune
paadeda Yesulo samastamu - samastamu Yese
2. Mannu shodhana shrama - nedu nammakam
mundu ardha rakshana - nedu sampoornam munnu viduvani pattu - nedesu nan batten poorvamu ne nastiram - nedu stiramaithi “Sarvamulo”
3. Munnu naa prayatnamu - nedu praardhana poorva mentho jaagratha - nedathani shraddha munnu naadu korika - nedesu maata
poorva madugu chunduta - nedu samstuti “Sarvamulo”
4. Munnu naa paniyadi - ikanu thanapani munnu thananu vaaditin nedu nan vaadunu
munnu shakhti korithin - nedu shakhtune
munnu naakai chesitin - nedu thanake “Sarvamulo”
5. Munnu Yesunu koritin - naa vaadaye nedu munnu jyotuluga nunde - ne dentho kaanthi munnu chaavu gorithi - nedu thana raakan
naa nireekshana lella - stiramaayenu “Sarvamulo”


. 524.Yesu aatma priyudaa  || యేసూ, ఆత్మ ప్రియుడా
Psalm 27:9
Jesus lover of my soul
1. Yesu aatma priyudaa - ninnu naashrayinchiti
levagaa darangamul - gaali vaana kottagaa jeeva
baadhalannitan nannu daachu rakshakaa nannu
nadpi revunan - aatma jerchu meethudan
2. Dikkuleni yaatmaku - vere praapu ledika
nontigaanu vidvaka - nannu yaadarinchu mee
ninne nammi yuntini - neeve naa sahaayamu
kaapuleni naa thalan - needu rekka krammanee
3. Kristu ninu gorudun - dorku nanni nee kadan
padda heenu neththu mee - swastaparchu rogulan
nyaaya shudda naamamu - neede nenu paapini
nenu paapa poornudan - neevu prema roopivi
4. Paapa mella maanpagaa - needu prema chaalunu
maanpu neellu naa yedan - shuddi cheyagaa nimmu
neevu jeeva ootavu - thraaga nimmu nee darin
putti naadu naatmalo - nella vela paarumee


. 525.Naa prema raajukapari || నా ప్రేమరాజు కాపరి
Psalm 23:1
The king of love my Shepherd is
1. Naa prema raajukapari - nannentho preminchunu - ee raaju vaada nainacho - naa ketti lemi ledu
2. Poshinchi naadu naatmaku - jeevampu neeti nitchun - poshinchu daani nityamun jeevaahaarambu thonu
3. Ne thappu throvanundagaa - rakshimpa vedake nannu - modambutho kanugonen - nan mandalona jerchen
4. Paatalam yokka cheekati - nan bheeti parcha bodu - naa daapu nunda kristesu - naa mundu nilchun silva
5. Naa drustilo nahaaramu - siddambu
jethu veevu - nee shuddha premaanandamul - paaren rakshimpa nannu
6. Nee manchi naijambo prabhoo
nirathambu nilchun stotrinthu ninnu
nee intan - O kaapari naa Yesu


. 526.Daiva prema pridviloni || దైవ ప్రేమ పృథ్విలోని
Eph, 3:19
Love divine, all loves excelling
1. Daiva prema pridviloni - yannitini minchunu
Yesu maalo nivasinchu - madi maa vimukhtiye
nee kamoolya prema yundu - neevu prema moortive
nee daasula mainamammu grupato rakshinchumu
2. Mammu samrakshinchu shakhti - nee kundu maa
prabhuvaa - yenna denna deni needu sannidini baayamu
nin stutinchu chundi memu - sarvadaa sevintumu
nin braardhinchi poorna prema - me matishayintumu
3. Krothagaa mammu srujinchi - paapa mella baapumu
maaku swastata nosangi - goppa rakshana joopumu
bhakhti yabhi vruddhi pondi - swarga mandu
jeragaa vintanondi prema stuti nee karpintu mepudu


. 527.Immuga nadipinchitivi || ఇమ్ముగ నడిపించితివి
1 Chr 28:20; Neh 6:16; Num 13:24
Pyar se Tu lekar aya
Pallavi : Immuga nadipinchitivi nemmadigala ee stalamunaku prabhoo
1. Maakunna stalamu irukaniyoo neeku moralidagaa mariyoka stalamu maa kosagitivi nee krupakai stutulu
2. Balaparachi mari dhairyamu nitchi abhayamu nitchitivi - ila nee mandiramunu nirmimpa janulanu koorchitivi “Immuga”
3. Prabhuvaa neekai nirmimpabadina nee mandira ghanatha sakala desha nivaasula yandu bhasilla goritivi “Immuga”
4. Mee madyalo naa Aatma yunnadani selavitchina Yesu prabhuvaa maaku thodai
yundi pani jariginchitivi “Immuga”
5. Pushkalamai bahujala maya maina thaavuku
thechitivi eshkolu draaksha phalamuluga
phaliyimpa goritivi “Immuga”
6. Anya janulu bahu aashcharya padiri nee ghana
kaaryamukai gurtinchirigaa nee adbutamulu
devaa stotramulu “Immuga”
7. Vendi bangaaramu lanniyu neevi dandiga
nitchedavu menduga needu melula korakai
Halleluya paadedamu “Immuga”


. 528.Anananda mahaanandam || ఆనంద మహానందం ప్రభువే

goppaanandam kummarinchunu madilo
paramu nundi paapi naligi nappude
2. Aanandinchudane prabhuve paramanduna
mee perul gorrepilla jeevagrandha mandu
vraaya badi yunnavani
3. Nee sannidhi yande kalavu nitya
santoshamulu - neechittamu neraverchu
vaarellaru anandichedaru sadaa
4. Idi varakunu meeremiyunu adugaledu
nannu - mee santoshamu paripoornamagu natlu
adigi pondu manenu
5. Yehovaa vimochinchina vare paatalu
paadi shiramulapai nitya santasamu
gala vaarai vachedaru
6. Aayana korakavamaanamunu mari
nindaku paatrulamu thana vaakyamevvari madiyandunduno
santoshinturu migula
7. Aatmalu rakshimpa badina adhikamugaa
santasinchu sarvakaalamu santoshamu
kaligi Halleluya paadedamu

. 530.Melkonumaa melkonumaa || మేల్కొనుమా మేల్కొనుమా

Yese nudivenu O priyudaa melkonumaa melkonumaa

prabhuni yokka chittambemo kaala viluvanu yerigi
Melkonumaa "Yese"
2. Nammajaala mee lokamunu
nee jeeva mepaatidi
samasthambu vyardhambegaa
praardhinchu maa "Yese"
3. Thappudu bodhalanundi
bhadra parachu konumu neevu
eppudu prabhu istahmunu
neraverchu maa "Yese"
4. Aaveshamu vyardhambegaa

ahankaara garvamu nundi
thappinchuko "Yese"

yeduru chooda valenu neevu
bhaasuramugaa thanatho
vella siddha padumaa "Yese"


. 531.Adbutha deevenalu prabhuvaa  || అద్భుత దీవెనలు

1. Maanavuni chesinaavu nee swantha
roopamunaku nee kistulamugaa brathiki
deevena lenno pondedamu "Adbutha"
2. Nootana janma valana aasheervaadamulu
dorike shaapamunu doora parachi
sarvambu krotha jese "Adbutha"
3. Lokamunundi verai siluvanu moya
valenu appude prabhu deevinchu
swaastyamunu gaanthu mentho "Adbutha"
4. Thana sutulu gaanu meligi - thana
chittamandu nilichi jeeva jalamunu
pondi deevena lenno pondedamu "Adbutha"
5. Aatmeeyamuga nadichi shareera
kriyalanu vidichi aayana swaramu
vinuchu - deevena lenno pondedamu "Adbutha"
6. Aasheervaadamula koraku piluvabadi
yunna manamu aajnalanu neraverchinacho
deevena lenno pondedamu "Adbutha"


. 532.Kristuni choochuchu saagi velledanu || క్రీస్తుని చూచుచు సాగివెళ్ళెదను
Heb. 12:1,2
Masih ko dekhkar age barhun main
1. Kristuni choochuchu saagi velledanu - sionu
yaatralo lokamun vidichi cherukondunu mahima
deshamun kristuni anugrahamulo surakshitha
hastamulalo mahaanandamutho stutinchuchu
cherudu naa deshamun
Pallavi : Entho sundara jeevithamu - mahimatho
nindinadi sadaa sarvadaa kristuthonundi
mahima parachedanu - mahimalo nundedanu
2. Dukkha shramalalo nannu rakshinchu daaguchotu
aayane sankataklesha pareekshalalo jayamu pondedanu
prabhunikai jeevinchedanu aayana
adugu jaadalalo aatma praana shareeramularpinchi
aayananu sevinthunu
3. Yaatrikudanu ee jagamandu - paravaasinaithi
nenu - swalpa jeevithamu bhuviyandu gadipi -
cherudun aa deshamun - naakai vijnaapanamu
cheyu - mahaa yaajakudu Yesunitho thodi vaarasudanai
aayanatho - nityamu eledanu


. 533.Velledamu koodi velledamu || వెళ్ళెదము కూడి వెళ్ళెదము
2 Peter 3:13
Ao chalen ham milkar chalen
Pallavi : Velledamu koodi velledamu
shresta deshamunu cherutaku -
neethi nivasinchunu anduna
1. Bhayamunu kaligi brathikedamu - paradeshulamani yerugavale - praveshinchavale vishraantilo -
thappi podumu marachinacho
2. Prabhuvaajnalanu paalinchutaku - prayaasa
padedamu manamilalo padilamugaa antamu varaku
padipokundaa choochukondumu
3. Prabhuvu mana kappaginchinavi - pattukoni
manamundedamu - dustuni baarini thappinchuko
dochukona nivvaku makutamu
4. Suluvugaa uriyoddu pratipaapamun -
sampoornamuganu tholaginchuchu
sahanamuthoda parugethuchu -
swarga deshamu cheravalen
5. Sampoornatha ponda saagedamu -
samarpinchukoni poornamugaa
sahinchina kastadukkhamulu -
bahugaa phala mondedamu


. 534.Oh prabhuvaa ne daari tholagithi  || ఓ ప్రభువా నే దారి తొలగితి
bhula bhatka dur main
Pallavi : Oh prabhuvaa ne daari tholagithi
nee sharanu jochitini - nee premanu ponditini
1. Naa paapamula ne noppu koni
pashchaataapa paditini - paapa kshamaapana
kalige
2. Prabhu Yesu nee rakhtamu dwaaraa
prayashchittamu jesitivi - kaduga baditini nenu
3. Nee rkhtamutho naa madikadigi - paapa
runamu theerchitivi - swatantruni jesitivi
4. Nee rakhtamuche paapamu tholage - rakshana
ne ponditini - paapa daagulanu thudiche
5. Nee rakhtamuche naa shiksha tholage
bandhakamula thenchitivi - nirdhoshigaa theerchitivi
6. Nee rakhtamuche sahavaasamunu paripoornatha
nondutaku - nanu vijayuni jesitivi


. 535.Ee loka yaatralo ne || ఈ లోక యాత్రలో నే

Duniya ke is safar men
Pallavi : Ee loka yaatralo ne saagu chunda (2)

ainanu kristesu naa thoda nundu (2)
1. Jeevitha yaathra yentho katihnamu (2)
ghorandhakaara thuphaanu lunnavi (2)
abhyantharamulu yennenno undu (2)
kaayu vaarevaru rakshinchedevaru (2) “Ee loka”
2. Hrudayamu shuddi parachu konnaanu
naa chethu lentho parishudda paracha
anukonani reeti niraasha vachchi
naa jeevitamunu naashana parache “Ee loka”
3. Neeve aashrayam kristesu prabhuvaa
anudinamu nannu aadarinchedavu
neetho unnaanu viduva ledanedu
nee prema madhura swaramu vinnaanu “Ee loka”
4. Ee anubhavamutho ne nadachu kondu
priya Yesu vaipu nenu choochuchu
gatamu nantha nenu marachi poyedanu
kanneeru thuduchu naa priya prabhuvu “Ee loka”
5. Thodai yundedavu anthamu varaku
neevu viduvavu andaru vidachinanu
nootana balamu naa kosagedavu
ne stiramuga nunda nee korika idiye “Ee loka”


. 536.Aadi premanu vidachi pettithivaa  || ఆది ప్రేమను విడచిపెట్టితివా
John -21:15
Kya tu pahla prem ab chhora hai
Pallavi : Aadi premanu vidachi pettithivaa
oh naadu priyudaa
maadiriga jeevincha maanitivaa (2)
1. Neeve naa rakshakuda vaniyu
devuni kreestunda vaniyu
nishchayamuga oppukontivi
swantha panulaku saagi potivi          "Aadi prema"
2. Siluva moyuchu Yesu prabhuke
kaala mella seva cheyuchu
ella prajalaku saakshyamitchuchu
velledanani palikitivi gaa                    "Aadi prema"
3. Manushya sangatulanu thalanchi
manu shyechalaku longi poyi
Yesu prabhuni anumaaninchi
dhana mosambulo chikku kontivi      "Aadi prema"
4. Emi thini thraagu chunduno
emi dharinchudunoyani
namma katwamu kolpoyi
ammu kontivaa needu prabhuni       "Aadi prema"
5. Meda middela polamu aastula
pudami nika nenno ghanathalaku
idiye samayamani thalanchi
needu prabhu nedirinchi poduvaa    "Aadi prema"
6. Yesu kreestuni seva yandu
emi koduvanu choochi itlu
maarchu kontivi needu nadathanu
naadhu desudu edchu chunde           "Aadi prema"
7. Needu deepamu inka ilalo
aari povaka munde nerigi
saadhuvai praardhinchu Yesuni
aadi prematho seva jeyumu               "Aadi prema"


. 537.Devunitho sahapaati  || దేవునితో సహపాటి

Ishwar ke sath sahkarmi aur
Pallavi : Devunitho sahapaati paalivaariganu
jese thodivaarasulanugaa manalanu
prabhu jesenugaa
1. Dushta lokamunundi adbuthamugaa
rakshinche amoolya vaghdaanamu litchi
daiva swabhaava mosagenugaa "Devuni"
2. Daiva velugunu pondi daivaatmalo paalu
pondi divya vaakyamunu pondi
divini ruchi choochitimi "Devuni"
3. Prabhu parishuddathalo paalivaara -
magunatlu sakala shramala paalai
daivashiksha nonditimi "Devuni"
4. Paraloka pilupunandu paali vaarigaanu
jese thana inti vaarinigaa jeya
manala nerparache "Devuni"
5. Thandrini stutinchedamu yogyulugaa
mamujese parishuddula swaastyamulo
paali vaarigaa jese "Devuni"
6. Kristulo paali vaarai kristu sugunamulanu
pondi drudamugaa nilichedamu
pattu vadalaka manamu "Devuni"
7. Raabovu mahimayandu paalivaaramou
manamu prabhu selavitchenugaa priyulanu
melkolpedamu "Devuni"


. 538.Nishchayamuga ninnu deevinchedanu || నిశ్చయముగ నిన్ను దీవించెదను
Gen.-12:2,3:, 17:2-6
Ashish ke upar ashish tujh ko dunga
Pallavi : Nishchayamuga ninnu deevinchedanu (2)
nishchayamuga ninnu vruddi pondintun (2)
1. Pratyakshamai pilikenuga prabhuvu sarvashakhtigala
Yehovaanu nenu naa sannidhin nirdhoshiga
nadachina - neetho nibhandhana niyamintunu "Nishch"
2. Nee santaanamunu deevinchi - ninnu phaliyimpa
jesedanu - neelo nundi janamulu vachunu -
neetho nibandhana stiraparathun "Nishch"
3. Yuga yugamulaku neeku devudanu - kaanaanu deshamu
nee kosagedanu - nitya swaastyamunu
nee kosagedanu - neelo mahima ne pondedanu "Nishch"
4. Goppa janamugaa jeseda ninnu - nishchayamugaa
aasheervadintun - nee naamamunu goppa jesedanu
aasheervaadamuga jesedanu "Nishch"
5. Ninnaasheerva dinchu vaarini - nenu aasheerva -
dinchedanu - dooshinchu vaarini ne shapinchedanu nee
dwaraa deevimpa badedaru "Nishch"


. 539.Yesu manatho nundaga || యేసు మనతోనుండగ
Acts - 4:13
Yishu Prabhu sath ab hai
Pallavi : Yesu manatho nundaga dairyamutho
saaguchu katihna maargamainanu
venukaku thirugamu
1. Paatha sangatulanniyu gatinche marala
raavuga - Yesu nandu kroththavai nootanamuga
nadupunu - Yesu prabhuni yaajnalu adbuthamuga
dorikenu parama darshana mandundi
tholagi pomu yennadu "Yesu"
2. Saitaanu shareeramu lokamutho poraaduchu
yentha krayamu nainanu santoshamuga
chellintumu - yuddha mandu jayamonda
prabhuni shakhti pondedam - Yesu jayamu
ponduchu saataanu raajya manachedam "Yesu"
3. Dukkha roga baadhalu kaligina chintinchaka
Yesu naama manduna pondedamu
shakhtini - alpa kaalayaatralo gonugu
sanugu lundaka prati paristiti yandu
thrupti chendi yundumu "Yesu"
4. Kristu Yesu manasune manamu kaligi -
yundamu - eershya krodha virodhamul
vidichi prema choopedam - naagati meeda
chethini unchi venuka tirugamu - Yesu vaipu
choochuchu aayana thoda nadachedam “Yesu”
5. Manalo paatha purushuni champedamu
siluvalo antaranga purushunandu balamunu
pondedamu - aatmeeya jeevitambulo unnatha
staanamu pondedam - shareera itchcha -
lanniyu anaga drokki vesedam “Yesu”
6. Vidachedam ee lokamu yaatra poorti chesedam parama
raajya manduna parama gruhamu
cheredam - Yesu prabhunu sandhinchedam
aanandamutho nindedam - bahumaanamulu pondedam
sadaa aayanatho nundedam “Yesu”


. 540.Prabhuvaa chesitivi vaagdhanamulu || ప్రభువా చేసితివి వాగ్దానములు
Jer. 1:5
Prabhuji Tune hain ki Pratigyaen ham se
Pallavi : Prabhuvaa chesitivi vaagdhanamulu maatho
neraverchitivi bahu nerputhodan
sannuthinchedano prabhuvaa
1. Vedikitivi nannu nee vaakyamuche
thagina kaalamuna ninnu cheran tharuna -
mitchitivi sottani nannu nee putruni jeya
kadigitivi nee rakhtamutho “Prabhuvaa”
2. Baaludanu bhaavana valadantivi
bahu janambulaku Pravakhtagaa niyaminchitivi
garbhamunande roopinchina prabhoo
pedanaina nenu poojintun “Prabhuvaa”
3. Bhaya bheetilo naaku abayamu nitchi
vijrumbinchina virodhipai vijayamunitchi
kattanu naatanu naa notanu nee maata
nunchina prabhoo kirtintun “Prabhuvaa”
4. Mandira mahimanu hetchulonuncha
sainyaadhipati needu samaadhanamu
nitchi ee stalamunu needu shaantito nimpina
shaalemu raajaa stotrintun “Prabhuvaa”
5. Mosheku neevu maata nitchi natlu
adugidu prati stalamu lannitini
maakitchutaku parishuddatmatho nimpina
prabhuvaa palu maatalatho pranutintun “Prabhuvaa”
6. Iha para manduna sarvaadhi kaarivai shishyulaku
nee aajna nitchina aatma deva
yugaantamuna nee sannidi maato
nunnandulakai stutiyintun “Prabhuvaa”
7. Vardhilladantivi ye aayudhamun neeku
virodamubugaa roopinchinacho
nyaaya vimarshalo tharuna mitchitivi
nera staapana cheyan Halleluyaa “Prabhuvaa”


. 541.Aanandinchedamu Yehovaalo  || ఆనందించెదము యెహోవాలో
Isaiah 61:6-11
Harshit ham honge Yahowa men
Pallavi : Aanandinchedamu Yehovaalo atishayinchunu
maadu aatma rakshana vastramulatho Yehovaa
mammu - neeti vastramun dharimpa jese
1. Paradeshulu mammu prabhuvaa devaa - needu yaajaka
sevaku lanedaru jagamuna janamula bhagyambitchi -
prabhavinthu rantivi prabhaavamutho “Aanandin”
2. Annyulu chesina avamaanamunaku - pratigaa maaku
rettimpu ghanathanu nindaku pratigaa pondina
bhaagamu anubhavinchuchu harshintu rantivi “Aanandin”
3. Vaaru thamadu deshamunandu - rettimpu bhagamunaku
kartha louduru - nityaanandamu vaariki kalugunu -
ennadu vaarini viduva nantivi “Aanandin”
4. Nyaayamu cheyuta naa kentho preeti - annyaayapu
sothu naa kasahyamu - satyamu batti prati phala mitchuchu
nitya nibhandana cheseda nantivi “Aanandin”
5. Janamulaku vaari santati theliyunu - janamula madyanu
prasiddi nondunu - Yehovaa aasheervadinchina janamani
oppukonduru choochina vaaru “Aanandin”
6. Bhoomi molakanu molipinchu natlugaa - thotalo
molichina viththanamu vale - janamula yeduta prabhu
Yehovaa - neethi stotramulanu ujjeevimpa jeyunu“Aanandin”
7. Kristu nandu maakitchina yatti - aatma bandhita prati
aasheessulakai sarvonnathudaa sannutinchuchu -
Halleluya stotramul aaropintumu “Aanandin”


. 542.Lellemmu Siyonu - dhariyinchumu || లేలెమ్ము సీయోను - ధరియించుము
Isaiah 52:1, Isaiah 60:1, Eze. 36:11
Jag jag ab he Siyyon
Pallavi : Lellemmu Siyonu - dhariyinchumu nee balamu
sundara vastramula dharinchu -
parishudda pattanamaa -
1. Nishkalanka Yerushalemaa - inkennatiki
nee madyaku sunnathi pondani apavitrulunu -
loniki raarennadunu “Lelemmu”
2. Lemmu neevu thejarillumu - velugu neeku
vachchiyunnadi - Yehovaa mahima nee meeda -
udayinchunu lelemmu “Lelemmu”
3. Manushyulanu pashuvulanu - vistarimpa
jesedanu abhivruddi nondunu apoorvamuga -
poorvastaanamulo ninnunthun “Lelemmu”
4. Munipatikante adhikamaina - melu neeku
kalugajetunu apudu neevu Yehovaa nenani -
vivaramugaa nerigedavu “Lelemmu”
5. Anduchetane cheppuchunnadu - nidrinche
neevu melukonumu mrutulalonundi
lechirammu prakaashinchunu kristu “Lelemmu”


. 543.Oh ishraayelu - needu bhagyamentho || ఓ ఇశ్రాయేలు - నీదు భాగ్యమెంతో
Pallavi : Oh ishraayelu - needu bhagyamentho
goppadi - Yehovaa rakshinchina
ninnu polina - vaadu evvadu ?

Yehovaa devude palken “Oh”
2. Naa nibhandhananu ne raddu paracha
nane gadaa naa nota nundi vellina
maatanu maarcha nane gadaa “Oh”
3. Sarvonnathuni raajyamu shashwatambu
nikkamu tholagi podu ennadu
layamu kaadu ennadu “Oh”
4. Nee mandira samruddhilo vaariki thrupti
galadu - nee aananda pravaahamulo -
neevu thraaginchu chunnaavu “Oh”
5. Neevu bhaya padakumu - baadhinchu
vaaru raakundanu dooramugaa nunchi
yunnaanu - neeku thodai yunnanu “Oh”


. 544.Naa jeevitha saagaramuna || నా జీవిత సాగరమున

. 546.Yehovaye manadevudu – marpulenivadu  || యెహోవాయే మనదేవుడు - మార్పులేనివాడు

. 549.Samadhanamu – devuni samadhanamu || సమాధానము - దేవుని సమాధానము

. 550.Yehova vimocincina vare || యెహోవా విమోచించిన వారె

3. Gruddiki kannulu cevitiki cevulu - kuntini gentedi duppiga jeya

4. Payaninturu varu raja margamuna - apavitrulu pojalaranduna
undadaccota e marga rajunu - parisuddha darilo paramagitamuto || Yehova ||
5. Bhayapadavaladani abhayambicci - varini raksimpa vegameraga

6. Nityamu dahincu agnijvalalalo - nundagajalinavaru evaru

7. Nitini buni yadardhamuga - vidina papalabhamunu
nityamu nilucu siyonu puriki - mudamuna jeri stutintuvu || Yehova ||
8. Unnata parvata silale vaniki - balamaina mahakotaga kaga
koduvenundadu tana aharamunu - panamunaku halleluya || Yehova ||


. 551.Devudehova divinci || దేవుడెహోవా దీవించి

. 552.Yehovanu nammukonu manavulu || యెహోవాను నమ్ముకొను మానవులు

adi ghoramaina dustatvamainadi - dini neruguvarevvaru 2
